
-----title
吉安（吉州） (出生地)
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年5月2日</a>　本年文天祥出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1239')">1237-1239年</a>　居家庐陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　入蒙学，从胡观洲习童子业。后又从曾秀峰、王东庐、朱约斋、业朱植、曾深甫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年5月9日</a>　从弟天瑞生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　三弟霆孙生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1241&endYear=1241')">1241年</a>　居家庐陵，习书塾，时江万里创办白鹭洲书院。后文天祥入读该书院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1242&endYear=1242')">1242年</a>　居家，习书塾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年</a>　游乡校，见先贤欧阳修、杨邦乂及胡铨像，慨然发誓“殁不俎豆其间，非夫也！”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1245')">1244-1245年</a>　居家庐陵，习书塾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　本年祖父时用殁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　居家庐陵，习书塾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>　居家庐陵，从父亲革斋先生学习。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年5月20日</a>　四弟文璋出生。初名天麟，字宋仁，晚字稚圭，号文堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1252')">1250-1252年</a>　居家庐陵读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1253&endYear=1253')">1253年</a>　本年乡校试，以《中道狂狷乡原如何》论题夺冠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　居家庐陵读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　春，肄业白鹭洲书院，深造欧阳守道门下。时刘辰翁、邓光荐同在。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　本年与弟文璧同举乡贡士。三弟霆孙逝世。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='99956576d4f74e308ef07eff2e44f841_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("99956576d4f74e308ef07eff2e44f841");'><span id='99956576d4f74e308ef07eff2e44f841_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年7月24日</a>　本日奉父亲革斋先生灵柩到达庐陵故里。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年7月25日</a>　本日朝廷立进士题名碑石于礼部贡院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年9月9日</a>　葬父于庐陵本乡敬佛源，后改葬泰和，居家守制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年8月</a>　右丞相丁大全致函求仕，辞谢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1258&endYear=1258')">1258年9月</a>　九月，为刘辰翁族叔刘良臣撰写楼记和族谱序。作品：《小腀读书楼记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（“秋”月据刘宗彬《刘辰翁年谱》第59页。《全宋文》不存该文。）</span>《小腀芳径甘溪刘氏初修通谱序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》不存该文。）</span><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5d540dfcb36e413188c1bd32dc2c20da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5d540dfcb36e413188c1bd32dc2c20da");'><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1260&endYear=1260')">1260年</a>　道士朱山月来访，以革斋先生遗墨相赠，文天祥有跋。作品：《敬书先人题洞岩观遗墨后》<div id='poem_1320340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320340' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_0_1320340_comment'></div>后十五年，知观任道士始摹本以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320340_comment'></div>又越三年，以次道士朱山月复为轴以相遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320340_comment'></div>维先君子天韵冲逸，神情简旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320340_comment'></div>使一日脱人事之累，黄冠野服，逍遥林下，真所甘心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320340_comment'></div>为子不德，使先志不获遂，捧轴却立，为之泫然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1320340_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='poem_sentence_2_58943'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年</a>　居家庐陵守心制。为江万里四丐祠抗贾似道。有书问候。作品：《通江参政古心书》<div id='poem_1319934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通江参政古心书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1266年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319934")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319934'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319934'>某即时甘雨，共惟宫使大参相公先生芝山清逸，珍馆宴超，天相有道，钧候动止多福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319934_comment'></div>某昨岁获走一介诣舍人门下，伏蒙钧念，劳苦有加，祗服训辞，至今亹亹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319934_comment'></div>俯仰山林，感慨年岁，又若是其阔疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319934_comment'></div>某官百年几见，一代共宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319934_comment'></div>司马居洛而相天子，活百姓，都人西其首而望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319934_comment'></div>张紫岩杜门白首，而嗣皇嗟叹用晚，倚之以向中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319934_comment'></div>先生今其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319934_comment'></div>上方举元祐故事，勤于梦卜，旦夕爰立，言人人同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319934_comment'></div>先生不以此觊于当世，而当世以此祈于先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319934_comment'></div>惟先生重爱眠食，以幸世道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319934_comment'></div>某屏伏田野，蒙赖钧天之庇，守先人坟墓，幸无阙状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319934_comment'></div>追惟两年间，口语横出，先生进而庙堂，退而江湖，德于其人，如出一日，传所谓生死肉骨之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319934_comment'></div>报答己知，言语抑末，倾竭犬马，尚庶几于门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319934_comment'></div>专人上状，百拜起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319934_comment'></div>衮舄皇皇，未遑纳拜，心之沄沄，如此江水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319934_comment'></div>仰乞钧照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1319934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年</a>　于庐陵得知文璧弟为马光祖推举，改官瑞州新昌县，有诗记之。作品：《别弟赴新昌》<div id='poem_59102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_4_59102'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59102_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1266&endYear=1266')">1266年</a>　春，邀请友人来文山赏乐。作品：《与胡端逸书》<div id='poem_1319956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与胡端逸书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1266年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319956")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319956'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319956'>自别后，日在山间搜奇剔怪，得二所，曰「闳微」，曰「上下四方之宇」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319956_comment'></div>幽闲旷邈，超伟轩张，其奇又在中矶两峰之间之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319956_comment'></div>君再来，足以抵掌大笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319956_comment'></div>「翠晚」又改曰「浮岚暖翠」，「钓雪」改曰「六月雪」，「特立」改曰「至大至刚以直」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319956_comment'></div>我非好怪，地适足以当之，君谓如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319956_comment'></div>新昌弟一介至门，馆谷之议谐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319956_comment'></div>专人导其来庭下，请君涖盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319956_comment'></div>江南春小，天和景明，山灵川后，毕献万状，欣然有应接佳客之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319956_comment'></div>不远二百里，杖屦容与乎其间，不亦可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319956_comment'></div>凌遽信笔，未究欲言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1319956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_4_1319934_comment'></div>张紫岩杜门白首，而嗣皇嗟叹用晚，倚之以向中原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319934_comment'></div>先生今其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319934_comment'></div>上方举元祐故事，勤于梦卜，旦夕爰立，言人人同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319934_comment'></div>先生不以此觊于当世，而当世以此祈于先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319934_comment'></div>惟先生重爱眠食，以幸世道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319934_comment'></div>某屏伏田野，蒙赖钧天之庇，守先人坟墓，幸无阙状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319934_comment'></div>追惟两年间，口语横出，先生进而庙堂，退而江湖，德于其人，如出一日，传所谓生死肉骨之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319934_comment'></div>报答己知，言语抑末，倾竭犬马，尚庶几于门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319934_comment'></div>专人上状，百拜起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319934_comment'></div>衮舄皇皇，未遑纳拜，心之沄沄，如此江水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319934_comment'></div>仰乞钧照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1319934_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1319944' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319944' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319944?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回衢教曾凤先生书<span class='inlineComment2'>（字朝阳，号秀峰。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319944")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319944_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319944'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319944'>某数月于师门极间阔，顾山水荒唐，不自知年岁之运运，阙礼多矣，尚庶几先生索之于形骸之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319944_comment'></div>别后得二子，丙寅戊戌，庚戌丙子，丁卯壬寅，甲午丙寅，命不知孰胜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319944_comment'></div>乍向风水，即得三地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319944_comment'></div>此须巨眼以为然则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319944_comment'></div>向牛肉坑所结砌者，今知其大谬，为弃屣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319944_comment'></div>深之昨所问馆，成否何所固必。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319944_comment'></div>新正诣清湖行礼，亦不见访，往往泥哭，则不歌之意，非有他也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319944_comment'></div>屋见说渐就绪，先生鼓舞倦矣，宜作意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319944_comment'></div>身事悠悠，何为行日，可得闻否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319944_comment'></div>春和景明，其间一造盘谷，亦可遍观先生所谓宝者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319944_comment'></div>更愿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1319944", 1319944, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>拨剔</span>而后来，一来须十日，乃可归尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319944_comment'></div>悉俟面赋，此不能尽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1319944_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1319949' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319949' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319949?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回邓县尉中甫书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1267年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319949")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319949_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319949'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319949'>某入山愈深，于所尊敬，嘻其阔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319949_comment'></div>前年足下以书议礼，得一往复，最后赐诲，迄今不能报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319949_comment'></div>论其形迹，何前之恭而后之倨欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319949_comment'></div>坡云：「人情重往复，不报生祸根」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319949_comment'></div>后山云：「一诗已经年，知子不我怨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319949_comment'></div>人之度量，固有相远，执事知我，宜可无前日之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319949_comment'></div>今通国识其用心，由其未定，而言辞之不可以已也如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319949_comment'></div>自其定者而观之，轻重铢两，固皆当然，言语文字，几乎闰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319949_comment'></div>昨书皆精义所发，卷为一通，谨而藏诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319949_comment'></div>后有作者，将为此兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319949_comment'></div>客从巽斋来，能言执事日从翁乐甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319949_comment'></div>因款客坐，亟亟援笔，写此悁结，授客以转之左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319949_comment'></div>学之不加，感慨年岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319949_comment'></div>山泽虽远，尚惠一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319949_comment'></div>临风拳拳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1319949_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1267&endYear=1267')">1267年9月</a>　除尚书左郎官，辞免不允。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5056d38f5b3142a1a3c2fe09165ef36f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5056d38f5b3142a1a3c2fe09165ef36f");'><span id='5056d38f5b3142a1a3c2fe09165ef36f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1269')">1268-1269年</a>，33-34岁</div><div id='5056d38f5b3142a1a3c2fe09165ef36f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年1月</a>　是月，因遭台臣黄庸奏，罢免归庐陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年1月8日</a>　为庐陵亡友萧明允撰墓志铭。作品：《萧明允墓志铭》<div id='poem_1320452' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320452' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320452?labeling=true' target='_blank'>萧明允墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1268年1月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320452")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320452_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320452'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320452'>君初名坚，字子固，后改应新，字明允，庐陵珠川人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320452_comment'></div>庐陵故多萧氏，而珠川亦望族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320452_comment'></div>君拔起其间，自幼岐嶷，长益崭绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320452_comment'></div>种绩文学，额额与逢掖争鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320452_comment'></div>三赴天子学，锐不少衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320452_comment'></div>气岸孤耸，与人棘棘不阿，号其读书室曰「介林」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320452_comment'></div>尝谓：「吾幸守先人庐，弗克规拓，是不肯堂」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320452_comment'></div>构楼其前，曰「逼云」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320452_comment'></div>复出其旁，相我攸宇，通之为园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320452_comment'></div>花竹横从，朋宾啸歌，翛然有物表之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320452_comment'></div>会予钓游荒闲，位置水石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320452_comment'></div>君时一造，沛然若自得，予以是知君所自负翘如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320452_comment'></div>咸淳二年十二月九日，以疾终，年四十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320452_comment'></div>曾祖炳文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320452_comment'></div>祖国老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320452_comment'></div>父景伯，妣李氏，继母曾氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320452_comment'></div>妃刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320452_comment'></div>男曰宋翁，女曰淑慧、淑慈、淑懿，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320452_comment'></div>卜以四年正月八日，归于淳化乡王田双园之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320452_comment'></div>前期，其弟至与其孤造门以铭请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320452_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1320452'>嗟予介林兮，孑孑而无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320452_comment'></div>大舆之壮兮，羌中道而折衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320452_comment'></div>意衣冠之虽葬兮，不能葬其英英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320452_comment'></div>瞻云山之莽苍兮，尚肮脏之如生。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1320452_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年5月14日</a>　与庐陵友人观文三大水，有记。作品：《文山观大水记》<div id='poem_1320408' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320408' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320408?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文山观大水记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1268年5月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320408")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320408_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320408'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320408'>自文山门而入，道万松下，至「天图画」，一江横其前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320408_comment'></div>行数百步，尽一岭，为松江亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320408_comment'></div>亭接堤二千尺，尽处为障东桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320408_comment'></div>桥外数十步为道体堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320408_comment'></div>自堂之右，循岭而登，为银湾，临江最高处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320408_comment'></div>银湾之上有亭曰「白石青崖」，曰「六月雪」，有桥曰「两峰之间」，而止焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320408_comment'></div>天图画居其西，两峰之间居其东，东西相望二三里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320408_comment'></div>此文山滨江一直之大槩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320408_comment'></div>戊辰岁，余自禁庐罢归，日往来徜徉其间，盖开山至是两年馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320408_comment'></div>五月十四日，大水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320408_comment'></div>报者至，时馆中有临川杜伯扬、义山萧敬夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320408_comment'></div>吾里之士以大学试，群走京师，惟孙子安未尝往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320408_comment'></div>辄呼马戒车，与二客疾驰观焉，而约子安后至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320408_comment'></div>未至天图画，其声如疾风暴雷，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1320408", 1320408, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>轰豗</span>震荡而不可御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320408_comment'></div>临岸侧目，不得往视，而隔江之秧畦菜陇，悉为洪流矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320408_comment'></div>及松江亭，亭之对为洲，洲故垤然隆起，及是，仅有洲顶而首尾俱失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320408_comment'></div>老松数十本，及水者争相跛曳，有偃蹇不伏之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320408_comment'></div>至障东桥，坐而面上游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320408_comment'></div>水从六月雪而下，如建瓴千万丈，汹涌澎湃，直送乎吾前，异哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320408_comment'></div>至道体堂，堂前石林立，旧浮出水面，如有力者一夜负去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320408_comment'></div>酒数行，使人候六月雪可进与否，围棋以待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320408_comment'></div>复命曰水断道，遂止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320408_comment'></div>如银湾，山势回曲，水至此而旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320408_comment'></div>前是立亭以据委折之会，乃不知一览东西二三里，而水之情状无一可逃遁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320408_comment'></div>故自今而言，则银湾遂为观澜之绝奇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320408_comment'></div>坐亭上，相与谐谑，赋唐律一章，纵其体状，期尽其气力，以庶几其万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320408_comment'></div>予曰：「风雨移三峡，雷霆擘两山」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320408_comment'></div>伯扬曰：「雷霆真自地中出，河汉莫从天上翻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320408_comment'></div>敬夫曰：「八风捲地翻雷穴，万甲从天骤雪騣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320408_comment'></div>惟子安素不作诗，闻吾三人语，有会于其中，辄拍手捋须，捧腹顿足，笑绝欲倒，盖有渊明之琴趣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320408_comment'></div>倚阑踰时，诡异卓绝之观不可终极，而渐告晚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320408_comment'></div>乃令车马从后，四人携手徐步而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320408_comment'></div>及家，而耳目眩颤，手足飞动，形神不自宁者久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320408_comment'></div>他日，予读《兰亭记》，见其感物兴怀，一欣一戚，随时变迁，予最爱其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320408_comment'></div>客曰：「羲之信非旷达者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320408_comment'></div>夫富贵贫贱屈伸得丧，皆有足乐，盖于其心，而境不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320408_comment'></div>欣于今而忘其前，欣于后则忘其今，前非有馀，后非不足，是故君子无入而不自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320408_comment'></div>岂以昔而乐，今而悲，而动心于俯仰之间哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320408_comment'></div>予怃然有间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320408_comment'></div>自予得此山，予之所欣日新而月异，不知其几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320408_comment'></div>人生适意耳，如今日所遇，霄壤间万物无以易此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320408_comment'></div>前之所欣所过者化，已不可追纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320408_comment'></div>予意夫后之所欣者至，则今之所欣者又忽焉忘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320408_comment'></div>故忽起奋笔，乘兴而为之记，且谂同游者发一噱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1320408_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1268&endYear=1268')">1268年11月9日</a>　冬至，除福建提刑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年</a>　江万里于三月诏为左丞相、兼枢密使后，有贺文。作品：《贺江左相启》<div id='poem_1320107' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320107' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320107?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺江左相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320107")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320107_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320107'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320107'>大老造朝，元台正席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320107_comment'></div>归公有衮绣，我来自东；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320107_comment'></div>用汝作盐梅，王置诸左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320107_comment'></div>三台明概，八表清夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320107_comment'></div>洪惟我朝相业之隆，莫如元祐家法之懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320107_comment'></div>潞公平章军国，司马实位昭文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320107_comment'></div>正献议论庙堂，微仲尝升左辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320107_comment'></div>或以学术真纯而辅君德，或以人物直谅而当帝心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320107_comment'></div>续遗响于先秦两汉之前，文章钜丽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320107_comment'></div>挺雄姿于黄河泰山之上，器量崇深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320107_comment'></div>此自古之难兼，盖于今而独见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320107_comment'></div>共惟某官行关百圣，名塞两间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320107_comment'></div>于前辈人期之以伊尹、傅说，今从学者尊之如韩愈、孟轲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320107_comment'></div>尚论公之平生，有报国之大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320107_comment'></div>以君子不用为我耻，以小人未退为己忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320107_comment'></div>童儿妇女知其血忱，缙绅大夫想其风采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320107_comment'></div>自其驱驰外服，出入中朝，洛中偃仰之年，江上经营之日，以致赞先皇之大政，参嗣圣之初元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320107_comment'></div>贤与不贤，一言定其可否；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320107_comment'></div>用或弗用，四海视以重轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320107_comment'></div>卓然一时人望之宗，展也三代王佐之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320107_comment'></div>属登庸之伊始，问梦卜以孰贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320107_comment'></div>朕安得斯人哉，固无踰老臣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320107_comment'></div>乃申帝指，乃穆师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320107_comment'></div>金瓯覆崔相之名，银信趣邺侯之觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320107_comment'></div>朝士举笏相贺，都民遮道聚观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320107_comment'></div>天子引见以劳归，东朝出馔以锡宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320107_comment'></div>遂由政路，径秉国钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320107_comment'></div>先天下而忧，斯能后天下而乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320107_comment'></div>有圣人之任，将以行圣人之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320107_comment'></div>莫难得者，海内相望之深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320107_comment'></div>最罕遇者，君子气类之合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320107_comment'></div>方今师维尚父，右举皋陶，赞襄于都俞之间，寅协于和同之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320107_comment'></div>钧无垠而播物，相天地，理阴阳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320107_comment'></div>鼎有足于承君，安国家，定社稷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320107_comment'></div>昔讲于洙泗者困道路之厄，而学于河汾者抱礼乐之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320107_comment'></div>道之行欤，时则可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320107_comment'></div>俾我后五三之盛，真吾儒千一之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320107_comment'></div>某猥在山栖，欣逢庭册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320107_comment'></div>亲见上下龙云之会，岂徒门阑燕雀之私？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320107_comment'></div>阳翟归耕，回首旧时之学士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320107_comment'></div>徂徕作颂，倾心今日之太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320107_comment'></div>庆抃情深，刊摩语浅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1320107_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年4月12日</a>　庐陵乡友刘元刚卒，作墓志铭。作品：《知昭州刘容斋墓志铭》<div id='poem_1320442' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320442' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320442?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知昭州刘容斋墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年4月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320442")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320442_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320442'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320442'>咸淳四年四月十二日，容斋先生刘公元刚卒于家，年八十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320442_comment'></div>先生官至郡守，死之日，几无以为歛，附于身者称家之有无，乡党之士莫不高先生之风而哀其志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320442_comment'></div>其邑子文天祥与人言，欷歔慷慨，重惧前辈言行久远<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1320442", 1320442, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>沈泯</span>，无以训来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320442_comment'></div>会其子昌孙以先生状来请铭，某虽不敏，其可以辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320442_comment'></div>先生字南夫，一字南强，世为吉州吉水县人，治毛氏《诗》，早为乡校知名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320442_comment'></div>嘉定十年入太学，后六年登进士第，授迪功郎、信州永丰县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320442_comment'></div>升从政郎，调静江军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320442_comment'></div>丁外艰，服除，差江州教授兼濂溪书院山长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320442_comment'></div>自故丞相董公槐、今丞相江公万里以下举亲民五员，淳祐五年班见，以通直郎知抚州崇仁县，县政以理，民以「佛子」为谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320442_comment'></div>先生奉母夫人在官，间日与其弟自提板舆，相羊为娱，邑人化之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320442_comment'></div>以忧去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320442_comment'></div>十年，通判鄂州，以磨勘转奉议郎、承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320442_comment'></div>董丞相当国，入为左藏东库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320442_comment'></div>时将荐先生试馆职，会董丞相去，不果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320442_comment'></div>初，东库日进会子纸若干，丁丞相以趣办为才，风有司顿增十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320442_comment'></div>先生以职力争，忤其意，展磨勘两年，出为泰州添差通判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320442_comment'></div>景定元年某月，差知昭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320442_comment'></div>皇上登极，转朝奉郎，适郡当次，称疾不果行，旨差主管建昌军仙都观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320442_comment'></div>居二年，再任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320442_comment'></div>自江上平，凡权奸用事所摈斥，朝廷奖拔殆尽，时论以先生为屈，未几诏还磨勘月日，骎骎向用，而先生前一月逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320442_comment'></div>呜呼，岂非命邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320442_comment'></div>早<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1320442", 1320442, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>刻意</span>词科，书无不读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320442_comment'></div>其馀佛老精言亦各深到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320442_comment'></div>平生居官，所至清谨，家无馀赀，萧然环堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320442_comment'></div>四方学者执经问字，相继于门，先生诱掖恳恳，不啻父兄之遇子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320442_comment'></div>尤工为文章，虽游戏之笔，鲜不奇古，江湖之士得品题一语，足自表于其徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320442_comment'></div>与人尽恭，应接终日无倦意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320442_comment'></div>客至，雅言之外，谈玄演空，闻者往往忘去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320442_comment'></div>世人以声利为门户，先生恶之，如恶恶臭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320442_comment'></div>登第垂五十年，郡县官吏知敬先生，不见其可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320442_comment'></div>出入不设<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1320442", 1320442, "Clauses/100/Comments/0")'>车徒</span>，间步行井陌中，不以为苦，甘心屡空，以至死而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320442_comment'></div>噫，此真所谓善人长者矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320442_comment'></div>曾祖致道，妣周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320442_comment'></div>祖圭，妣李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320442_comment'></div>考次朔，累赠至奉直大夫，妣陈氏、熊氏，俱赠恭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320442_comment'></div>妃涂氏，先十六年卒，赠安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320442_comment'></div>子男三人，昌孙其长也，次信孙、愚孙，皆蚤世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320442_comment'></div>女长夭，次适太学生陈应发，又次适进士胡渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320442_comment'></div>孙男一人，洵武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320442_comment'></div>女一人，许适龙氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320442_comment'></div>以某月某日葬某县某乡某里之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320442_comment'></div>遗墨有《诗》、《书》、《孝经》、《论语》、《孟子演义》若干卷，《词科类稿》若干卷，《容斋杂著》若干卷，《家庭谩录》若干卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320442_comment'></div>任左藏日，以《孝经》、《论语》、《孟子演义》上进，有旨降付资善堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320442_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1320442'>文彪彪，德恂恂，贵如单门，死如齐民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1320442_comment'></div>约而家，丰而身，我作铭诗，永怀古人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1320442_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年4月17日</a>　差知宁国府，辞免不允。作品：《辞免知宁国府状》<div id='poem_1319919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免知宁国府状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年4月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319919")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319919'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319919'>具位文某照会：伏准尚书省劄子：四月十七日三省同奉圣旨，文某差知宁国府，替朱应元缺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319919_comment'></div>起家超躐，望阙徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319919_comment'></div>伏念某实无他肠，粗有远志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319919_comment'></div>昔年忧国，冒当事任之难；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319919_comment'></div>数岁杜门，宁悔身谋之拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319919_comment'></div>属明良之胥庆，念岳牧之畴庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319919_comment'></div>曾谓栖迟，遽叨选用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319919_comment'></div>惟是某省愆已至，贬秩犹新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319919_comment'></div>虽公论至久而愈明，而丹书未谓之无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319919_comment'></div>傥不量于出处，是自速于颠隮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319919_comment'></div>欲望公朝特赐敷奏，收回成命，改畀丛祠，使某得以读书养亲，安身寡过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319919_comment'></div>他有驱驰之日，无非报效之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319919_comment'></div>所有省劄，已寄留吉州军资库，未敢祗受，须至申闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1319919_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='65bfa027d38e45c089ba12a090718860_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("65bfa027d38e45c089ba12a090718860");'><span id='65bfa027d38e45c089ba12a090718860_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1273')">1270-1273年</a>，35-38岁</div><div id='65bfa027d38e45c089ba12a090718860' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年9月13日</a>　本日抵达庐陵故居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年9月</a>　与吉州提举江万顷商讨赈灾事，有书信来往。作品：《知吉州提举万顷书  二通》其一。《知吉州提举万顷书  二通》其二。<div id='poem_1319983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与知吉州江提举万顷书<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1270年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319983")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319983'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319983'>某伏蒙公劄下问劝分，仰见岂弟父母，救民水火之盛心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319983_comment'></div>某实共邦人额手大赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319983_comment'></div>某所居里，凡千馀家，常年家中散米，一日不收钱，诸大家以次接续赈粜，可及三十日，隔一日粜，可当两月，此方尽可无饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319983_comment'></div>他时不待劝率，自是举行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319983_comment'></div>明年系紧要年分，或须使榜一申严之，至期却当取禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319983_comment'></div>但四境委有可忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319983_comment'></div>盖吾州从来以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1319983", 1319983, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>早稻</span>充民食，以晚稻充官租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319983_comment'></div>今年晚稻半亏，颗粒并是入官之数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319983_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1319983", 1319983, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>早稻</span>不过二三分，则是民食十减七八，此其所以皇皇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319983_comment'></div>近见多有趍龙泉、永新运籴者，觉彼二处米亦有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319983_comment'></div>县大夫各私其土，不肯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1319983", 1319983, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>透泄</span>，亦其不得已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319983_comment'></div>此须使司示以意向，使之斟酌放行，庶彼此可以均济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319983_comment'></div>最急莫如通赣州之米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319983_comment'></div>近同年李守惠书，自谓年谷中熟，米价日低。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319983_comment'></div>某尝答书云：「庐陵一歉，异于常年，田里憔悴，不堪举目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319983_comment'></div>惟章贡素无籴事，而得岁又偏，乡人颠顿者往往相率而趍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319983_comment'></div>治国民食关系，苟可通融，兼爱秦晋，公之惠也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319983_comment'></div>盖赣浮桥泄米之令素严，田吉号产米，而赣多山少田，故为赣计，不容旁及邻邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319983_comment'></div>今岁事既相反，又当通变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319983_comment'></div>此须古崖一书，与李守通情，俟得其要领，然后大榜境内，许人赴赣收籴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319983_comment'></div>此亦权宜之一策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319983_comment'></div>区区管见，姑复仁明，后有利便，又须陆续申控。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1319983_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　居庐陵家。作品：《赣州重修嘉济庙记》《赣州重修清献赵公祠堂记》<div id='poem_1320417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赣州重脩嘉济庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1271年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320417")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320417'>今天子咸淳六祀，大宗丞、权侍左郎官李雷应被旨知赣州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320417_comment'></div>赣地大而俗嚣，山宽而田狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320417_comment'></div>俗嚣故易以噪，田狭故易以饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320417_comment'></div>侯未至以为难，将至以为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320417_comment'></div>乃七月下车，膏雨霈流，嘉气坌集，民声大和，四郊以宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320417_comment'></div>侯悦，莫喻所从来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320417_comment'></div>百姓歌之曰：「我土沨沨，黍稷芃芃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320417_comment'></div>孰启我侯，我神之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320417_comment'></div>我氓蚩蚩，牛犊熙熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320417_comment'></div>孰相我侯，我神之威」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320417_comment'></div>侯惊，召父老进而问故曰：「是何神也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320417_comment'></div>父老相率告于庭曰：「州之东有庙曰『嘉济』，自秦汉以来，血食至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320417_comment'></div>我民司命，匪神其孰尸之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320417_comment'></div>侯恤然曰：「我何以得此于神哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320417_comment'></div>抑神实德我，我其有不致力于神」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320417_comment'></div>乃肃笾豆，乃洁牲牷，晨起诣庙，以谢以祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320417_comment'></div>既竣事，周视庭宇，不遑于宁，始建议营度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320417_comment'></div>刊木于厓，浮竹于津，厥材既坚，厥工惟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320417_comment'></div>植圮支仆，撤去庳陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320417_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1320417", 1320417, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>佣力</span>奔走，咸劝于事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320417_comment'></div>堂皇言言，廊庑严严，有门秩然，有亭翼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320417_comment'></div>于是神位具宜，庙制大备，王宫皇皇，衮冕裳衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320417_comment'></div>祠既毕，则以其馀脩道逵以便来游者，葺二浮梁以便绝江者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320417_comment'></div>钱奇二百万，粟奇二百硕，悉出侯所节缩，故役成而人不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320417_comment'></div>明年四月，侯除荆湖南路提点刑狱，未行，粟米在市，󵵳麦满野，鸡犬相闻，达于岭表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320417_comment'></div>讫侯去，视始至如一日焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320417_comment'></div>百姓复歌之曰：「奕奕庙貌，我侯新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320417_comment'></div>侯为我民，匪神是私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320417_comment'></div>田有稻粱，野无干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320417_comment'></div>微侯之赐，胡以室家？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320417_comment'></div>屡舞𠎣𠎣，伐鼓渊渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320417_comment'></div>何以报侯，万有千年」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320417_comment'></div>予时卧山中，州从事具本末来，属予言其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320417_comment'></div>予按祭法：能御大菑则祀之，能捍大患则祀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320417_comment'></div>神之为灵昭昭矣，谨叙次下方，纳诸庙门为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1320417_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1320416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赣州重修清献赵公祠堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1271年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320416")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320416'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320416'>郡所在祠先贤之为守者，守得祠以遗爱，然而百世之下，君子之泽有存焉者寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320416_comment'></div>而闻其风，为之兴起，尸而祝之，不谋同辞，识者于是上下世道而观其大节焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320416_comment'></div>故参知政事、赠太子少师清献赵公抃，历事仁宗、英宗、神宗，以忠亮纯直为时名臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320416_comment'></div>公尝治虔、治益、治杭、治越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320416_comment'></div>其政本之以清淡，行之以简易，宽不为弛，严不为残，使在汉氏，课功第能，当不在循吏下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320416_comment'></div>抑公所为大过人者，不宁惟是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320416_comment'></div>当王安石变更祖宗法，海内骚动，廷臣唯诺趋走，莫敢后先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320416_comment'></div>独与司马文正光、范忠文镇、唐质肃介<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1320416", 1320416, "Clauses/26/Comments/2")'>额额</span>争论，不少假借。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320416_comment'></div>至上疏言财利于事为轻，民心得失为重，不罢青苗使者，非宗社之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320416_comment'></div>公卒去位，小人相继用事，浊乱天经，蘖牙祸根，荆舒之罪，秽污简册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320416_comment'></div>「如有一个臣，断断猗无他技」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320416_comment'></div>中原遗老，炳然元龟，天下后世，感愤追想，犹凛凛有生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320416_comment'></div>呜呼，此其所谓大节，关系于世道治乱升降，而不可诬也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320416_comment'></div>咸淳六年，知赣州、大宗丞番阳李侯雷应以公尝辱为是邦，始至，访公祠所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320416_comment'></div>郡治故有祠，与濂溪并。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320416_comment'></div>自濂溪移祀于学，前守陈公宗礼始建公庙于城之东偏，岁时妥侑，习为故常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320416_comment'></div>屋弊且压，神不顾享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320416_comment'></div>侯慨然曰：「是不可惮改」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320416_comment'></div>会岁丰人和，庭无徵发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320416_comment'></div>于是栋楹栏槛之腐败挠折者，瓴甓丹雘之疏漏漶漫者，神位祭器之缺失不如礼者，所费俭约，一日新美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320416_comment'></div>又更为之门，俯临大衢，非徒侈观，使过者敬恭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320416_comment'></div>明年夏五落成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320416_comment'></div>侯时已除湘南刑狱使者，将行，走书属某记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320416_comment'></div>某惟吏道苟且，逐末忘本久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320416_comment'></div>侯之先公忠清有风裁于世，侯得之见闻，独能尊事文献，景行先哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320416_comment'></div>风示邦人，以绎教思，其渊源有自来哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320416_comment'></div>清献距今二百馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320416_comment'></div>赣石，公所凿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320416_comment'></div>章贡台，公所创也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320416_comment'></div>公之事远矣，而其山川犹有衣被其馀者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320416_comment'></div>赣人之思之曰：「公生而德泽在吾土，公之赐也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320416_comment'></div>公死而典刑在吾土，公之赐也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320416_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320416_comment'></div>公之在熙宁也，当时小人号为得志，富贵澌尽，终归无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320416_comment'></div>赣何地也，而公祠在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320416_comment'></div>后公而为赣者相望，亦岂无可以系去思者，而公之祠岿然灵光，何其懿也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320416_comment'></div>呜呼，士大夫之于当世，其大节可不谨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320416_comment'></div>可不谨哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1320416_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　居庐陵家。江万顷离吉州，有道别函。作品：《与知吉州江提举万顷》<span class='inlineComment2'>（题目由录者查询得知。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年11月9日</a>　居家庐陵。冬至日，除湖南运判。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1271&endYear=1271')">1271年</a>　居家庐陵。作品：《回宁国陈节容书》<div id='poem_1320006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回宁国陈节推容书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1271年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320006")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320006'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320006'>去年阙下拜书，稍得数数，未几，闻捧檄校文，不知陶铸何处人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320006_comment'></div>某自是即汰斥去，闭门深山，遂无复鳞鸿一日之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320006_comment'></div>忽使者来山中，欣得妙帖，见示《小录》，方知昨者衡鉴所向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320006_comment'></div>近想归舟荡漾彭蠡，吾知心正在香炉峰白云下耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320006_comment'></div>宣之弛征，执事首从臾之，幸而集事，仅足了吾辈之责，非相与为赐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320006_comment'></div>书来，乃知宣人以此为多，祠之以识其不忘之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320006_comment'></div>怵惕于孺子之入井，岂为内交要誉设？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320006_comment'></div>抑桐乡父老此意，亦能使人感激耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320006_comment'></div>宣为郡凋剧，极力扶持，幕画间想见劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320006_comment'></div>盘错纠结，以试利器，天下事正有赖于方来耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320006_comment'></div>某前冬一出，去秋一归，进退行藏，惟其所遇，而无心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320006_comment'></div>则今奉亲课子，弹琴读书，流水青山，悠然独往，不烦故人江云渭树之思也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320006_comment'></div>《史记》见贶，家藏本皆不及，尚当朝夕，以称所蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320006_comment'></div>《明善录》一部，谩侑归笺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320006_comment'></div>临墨驰溯之至<span class='inlineComment2'>（《文山全集》卷六。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320006_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1320006'>「想」上原有「思」字，据库本删。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1320006_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年5月2日</a>　居家庐陵。生日，与友人多有唱和。作品：《生日和聂吉甫 五月初二日》《生日和谢爱山长句 崧老,字伯华》《生日谢朱约山和来韵》《生日山中和萧敬夫韵》<div id='poem_59356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>生日和谢爱山长句<span class='inlineComment2'>（崧老，字伯华）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年5月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59356")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59356'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59356'>寓形落落大块间，嘘吸一气自往还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59356'>桑弧未了男子事，何能局促甘囚山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59356'>昔年此日作初度，宾客如云剧欢舞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59356'>今年避影却闭门，捧觞自寿白头母。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59356'>故人忆我能远来，虹光满袖生琼瑰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59356'>一杯相属慰岑寂，使我<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_59356", 59356, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>发笑</span>愁颜开。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59356'>簸扬且听箕张口，丈夫壮气须冲斗。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59356'>夜阑拂剑碧光<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>寒，握手相期出云表。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59356'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_59356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_59356'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_59356_0'>⑴ 韩本、四库本作花</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_59356_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_59357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>生日谢朱约山和来韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年5月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59357")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59357'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59357'>元丰五年正月日，洛中耆英佳话出。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59357'>当时韩公七十九，欢噱赓酬老吟笔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59357'>伟然冠剑照孔鸾，鲐背鸠杖蒲轮安。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59357'>韩公而下文宽夫，相高以寿不以官。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59357'>洛尘已随流水急，云仍相逢松下石。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59357'>顾我行辈真我来，兼谟<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作慕）</span>故事强安排。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59357'>约对青山共长久，醉歌要赛<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作赓）</span>滁州守。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59357'>愿随后社著深衣，阑风伏雨从是非。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59357'>便令携樽西墅去，山花山鸟为歌舞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59357'>招招瑶母来庭闱，拍手共笑偷桃儿。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59357'>吾山陂陀白云满，猿鹤司我北门管。<div id='poem_sentence_10_59357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59357'>紫霞隔断鸡犬声，下有琥珀滋长龄。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>生日山中和萧敬夫韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年5月2日）</span><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　六七月间，居家庐陵。身染疾病，至七月始愈。作品：《病中作》《又二绝》《又赋》五首其一。《又赋》五首其二。《又赋》五首其三。《又赋》五首其四。《又赋》五首其五。借道冠有赋。又赋（一番潮信过）病甚梦召至帝获宥觉而顿愈遂赋。病愈简刘小村 二首。回谢教授爱山四贴。<div id='poem_59297' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59297' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59297?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又二绝<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span href='/Writing/59213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病愈简刘小村<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59213")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_sentence_0_59213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59213'>古鼎龙团雪，虚檐麈尾春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59213_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59213'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59213_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59214?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59214_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59214'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59214'>倦馀心似醉，病起首如蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59214'>黄竹断桥雨，白蘋长笛风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59214'>仙仙鸥屡舞，咄咄雁书空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59214'>孤负秋来眼，闲挑爨下桐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59214'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59214_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1319965' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319965' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319965?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回谢教授爱山四帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319965")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319965_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319965'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319965'>虽块坐深山，于时高人韵士，鼎铛独无耳乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319965_comment'></div>载酒问奇，道之云远，徒有是心，而未之能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319965_comment'></div>不图五盐道院，屈居仙客，阶兰砌玉，与亭芝相照映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319965_comment'></div>每思吾仲取友必端，未尝不自叹独学之陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319965_comment'></div>手书宠贻，清扬流动，虽未见犹既见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319965_comment'></div>何时簪盍，慰此忡惙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319965_comment'></div>临风驰报，书不尽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319965_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1319965'>寒檐积雨，抖擞无悰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319965_comment'></div>得书而读之，昏眼为拭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319965_comment'></div>某落落白云间，一畴春绿，自饭吾犊，浮世荣辱事，付之山外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319965_comment'></div>褒惜所蒙，君言过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319965_comment'></div>然醴露醲郁，波及沟断，企瑞芝而遐眺，佩金兰之永好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319965_comment'></div>美人一方，书琴自适，为诵《停云》三过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319965_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1319965'>日于仲氏便价得书，振衣快读，恍焉眉宇之迫吾睫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319965_comment'></div>可人不来，苍苔满径，得无忘把酒看山时约耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319965_comment'></div>西风逼人，桂香浮动，天池鲲化，抟扶摇而上之，舍爱山其谁属魁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319965_comment'></div>卷纸一幅，纳之文房，衣被琳琅，腾翥光景，褚生辈亦将侈其逢矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319965_comment'></div>薄言占复，挂一漏万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319965_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1319965'>山中度日如年，落叶萧萧，凉月堕砌，起视寥泬，安得知己握手长吟，写胸中之耿耿，以相慰藉耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319965_comment'></div>杪秋馀热犹壮，二竖者虽相戏而不吾虐，予亦从其所为，仓扁辈未尝屑屑然也，久之不觉脱然去体，是又不治之治，有胜于剂饵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319965_comment'></div>宠贻手札，问劳渠渠，故道其所以然，而以复于执事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1319965_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　居家庐陵。作品：《吉州州学贡士庄记》《赣州兴国县安湖书院记》<div id='poem_1320405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吉州州学贡士庄记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320405")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320405'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320405'>物之在天地间，自铢粟以上，莫不有主名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320405_comment'></div>独贡士庄所储，以拟夫三岁大比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320405_comment'></div>士之送上春官者，有司不知谁宜得之，取什伯于千万，亦无敢自必为己得，其予夺之，殆有物焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320405_comment'></div>逸史称，隋末一书生，所居抵官库，有数万钱，欲取之，神人诃之曰：「此尉迟公钱也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320405_comment'></div>泉者，天之利器，惟天能以与人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320405_comment'></div>则夫任贡士庄者，殆为天守利器，以俟夫天之所以与人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320405_comment'></div>充是心以往，真无所为而为之，其为仁岂不至，而为义岂不尽乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320405_comment'></div>咸淳六年，简池赵君必礿来为庐陵教授，作兴斯文，教养毕具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320405_comment'></div>则按贡士庄之旧，稽其所出内，岁钱谷几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320405_comment'></div>庐陵士甲江右，一科数路，资送四五百人，裒多益寡，称物平施，末之云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320405_comment'></div>于是有增田之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320405_comment'></div>一之日置尹氏租，为米八十斛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320405_comment'></div>二之日置彭氏租，为米一千一百九十二斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320405_comment'></div>赵君犹以为未足，则曰：「传而益之，其来者之事哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320405_comment'></div>添差教授番阳程君申之继至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320405_comment'></div>相与诣郡，请蠲赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320405_comment'></div>吏持难易，阁弗下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320405_comment'></div>永嘉缪侯元德甫下车，二君申其请，侯慨然曰：「奈何与吾党校琐琐乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320405_comment'></div>复之不崇朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320405_comment'></div>予闻而异之，以为侯与广文之用心，皆所以奉天道之不及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320405_comment'></div>古之爵人，言必称天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320405_comment'></div>国家谨惜名器，自他蹊者悉名侥倖，惟进士科，使四方寒畯操觚而进，付得失于外有司，而定高下于殿陛之亲擢，公卿大夫繇此其选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320405_comment'></div>当是时，天子宰相一不得容心于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320405_comment'></div>予尝谓今世惟科举一事为有天道行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320405_comment'></div>士脩于家，试于乡，如探筹然，以信夫天命之所遭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320405_comment'></div>而为贡士计者，积仓裹粮，共其道路，先事而为之备，随天命之所与而后与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320405_comment'></div>是心也，岂复有内交要誉之私哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320405_comment'></div>予故曰：皆所以奉天道之不及者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320405_comment'></div>是宜书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320405_comment'></div>且夫取士于天下，将以为天下用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320405_comment'></div>人之常情，其穷也不为利疚，则其达也不可以非义屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320405_comment'></div>后之临大节，断大事，决非异时箪食豆羹见于色者之所能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320405_comment'></div>夫使郡国上其贤能，而汉人续食之意隐然寄于学校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320405_comment'></div>士得以直走行都，而无仆马后顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320405_comment'></div>所望于人也轻，则所以全于己也大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320405_comment'></div>是邦学者世修欧、周之业，人负胡、杨之气，如有用我，执此以往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320405_comment'></div>是举也，世道微有赖焉，盖益可书也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320405_comment'></div>是庄创始于尚书胡公槻，隶于学者米二千二百斛有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320405_comment'></div>前丞相叶公梦鼎为郡增六百三十斛有奇，前教官黄君恺伯增一千三百六十斛有奇，前赵侯典椯增四百一十斛有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320405_comment'></div>自二教创后，施君郁、郑君师皋增二百五十斛有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320405_comment'></div>合今所增，通为米六千一百斛有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320405_comment'></div>以学谕提点庄事，刘少南、张敏子云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320405_comment'></div>八年八月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1320405_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1320418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赣州兴国县安湖书院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1272年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320418")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320418'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320418'>赣兴国县夫子庙在治之北门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320418_comment'></div>县六乡，其五乡之人来游来歌，被服儒雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320418_comment'></div>东二百里曰衣锦乡，其民生长斗绝险寒，或为龙蛇，渎于邦经，有司黾勉，以惠文从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320418_comment'></div>咸淳八年，宣教郎临川何时来为宰，悯然曰：「使人不可化，则性命之道熄矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320418_comment'></div>顾邑校旷越不克施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320418_comment'></div>乃夏四月，即其地，得山水之胜，议建书堂，以风来学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320418_comment'></div>召其豪长，率励执事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320418_comment'></div>堂庭毕设，讲肄有位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320418_comment'></div>汇试馆下，录为生员凡二十八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320418_comment'></div>又拔其望四人为之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320418_comment'></div>冬十月，令率诸生以牲币荐于先圣先师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320418_comment'></div>樽俎旗章，等威孔严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320418_comment'></div>环观愕眙，屏息胥忭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320418_comment'></div>黧老妇子，转相传呼，然后翕然以儒者为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320418_comment'></div>令曰：「吾教可行矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320418_comment'></div>载命胥正，秩其比伍，家使有塾，人使有师，如党庠术序之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320418_comment'></div>置进学日记，令躬课其凡，督以无怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320418_comment'></div>又上诸府，改其乡曰「儒学」，植之风声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320418_comment'></div>于是山长谷荒，人是用劝，咸愿进向文事，率由训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320418_comment'></div>程传曰：「天地之道浸」，言化以渐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320418_comment'></div>风俗之积几千百年，而令一朝变之，固若是速欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320418_comment'></div>共惟国家五星聚奎，实开文明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320418_comment'></div>皇祖制诏，天下州县立学，所在表章儒先，复创书院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320418_comment'></div>三代以下，斯文彬彬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320418_comment'></div>先民有言，「地气自北而南」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320418_comment'></div>粤从衣冠正朔，启我吴会，自江以南，悉为邹鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320418_comment'></div>今也遐荒陋僻，沐浴教恩，如狂得瘳，如迷得呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320418_comment'></div>王泽之渗漉日深，地气之推移日至，此岂偶然之故哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320418_comment'></div>予于令为同年进士，适守是州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320418_comment'></div>今奉天子明训，以字民为职，能广学爱，宣德化，是为不辱威命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320418_comment'></div>将上其事于朝，复谂之诸生曰：「昔有文翁，兴学于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320418_comment'></div>受业博士，时则张叔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320418_comment'></div>学官弟子，畏而怀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320418_comment'></div>彼何人哉，叔兮叔兮」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320418_comment'></div>又进诸生之长谂之曰：「昔有文公，设教于潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320418_comment'></div>潮人赵德，以士见招。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320418_comment'></div>维文与行，倡于齐民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320418_comment'></div>其则不远，德哉若人」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320418_comment'></div>诸生拱而前曰：「某等幸生明世，惟师帅不鄙夷之，俾获有闻，虽不敏，敢不受教！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320418_comment'></div>请刻诸石，以诏百世」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320418_comment'></div>书院之制，前为燕居，直以杏坛，旁为堂，左先贤祠，祠后为直舍，缭斋以庑，不侈不隘，临溪为之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320418_comment'></div>堂名「絜矩」，斋名「笃志」、「求敏」、「明辨」「、主善」、「率性」、「成德」，其门总曰「安湖书院」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320418_comment'></div>某山中所题云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1320418_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1272&endYear=1272')">1272年</a>　居家庐陵。弟文璧签判宁海军，通判临安，军府称治。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年1月</a>　除湖南提刑，辞免不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年1月7日</a>　师欧阳守道卒，有祭悼文。作品：《祭欧阳巽斋先生文》<div id='poem_1320457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭欧阳巽斋先生文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年1月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320457")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320457'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320457'>维岁次癸酉正月乙卯朔，越七日辛酉，学生具位文某，谨致祭于故先生殿讲、大著、刑部巽斋欧阳公棺前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320457_comment'></div>呜呼，先生将安归邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320457_comment'></div>先生之学，如布帛菽粟，求为有益于世用，而不为高谈虚语，以自标榜于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320457_comment'></div>先生之文，如水之有源，如木之有本，与人臣言依于忠，与人子言依于孝，不为曼衍而支离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320457_comment'></div>先生之心，其真如赤子，宁使人谓我迂，宁使人谓我可欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320457_comment'></div>先生之德，其慈如父母，常恐一人寒，常恐一人饥，而宁使我无卓锥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320457_comment'></div>其与人也，如和风之着物，如醇醴之醉人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320457_comment'></div>及其义形于色，如秋霜夏日，有不可犯之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320457_comment'></div>其为性也，如槃水之静，如佩玉之徐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320457_comment'></div>及其赴人之急，如雷霆风雨互发而交驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320457_comment'></div>其持身也，如履冰，如奉盈，如处子之自洁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320457_comment'></div>及其为人也，发于诚心，摧山岳，沮金石，虽谤兴毁来，而不悔其所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320457_comment'></div>天子以为贤，缙绅以为善类，海内以为名儒，而学者以为师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320457_comment'></div>凤翔千仞，遥增击而去之，奈何一蹶而不复支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320457_comment'></div>以先生仁人之心，而不及试一郡，以行其惠爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320457_comment'></div>以先生作者之文，而不及登两制，以彷佛乎盘诰之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320457_comment'></div>以先生之论议，而不及与闻国家之大政令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320457_comment'></div>以先生之学术，而不及朝夕左右献纳而论思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320457_comment'></div>抑童而习之，白首纷如也，虽孔、孟圣且贤，犹不免与世而差池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320457_comment'></div>先生官二著不为小，年六十五不为夭，有子有孙，而又何憾于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320457_comment'></div>死而死耳，所以不死者，其文在名山大川，诏百世而奚疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320457_comment'></div>某弱冠登先生之门，先生爱某如子弟，某事先生如执经，盖有年于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320457_comment'></div>先生与他人言，或终日不当意，至某虽拂意逆志，莫不为之解颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320457_comment'></div>世有从师于千里，尚友于异代，而同人于门，适相值而不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320457_comment'></div>其死也，哀斯文之不幸，吊生民之无禄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320457_comment'></div>其葬也，只鸡斗饭，窃慕古人之义，匍匐奔走，泫然而哭吾私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320457_comment'></div>呜呼，已而已而！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320457_comment'></div>哀哉，尚享。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1320457_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年2月1日</a>　从里中士奉币载酒拜罗氏百岁母寿，有诗。作品：《庆罗氏祖母百岁》<div id='poem_59067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庆罗氏祖母百岁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59067")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59067'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59067'>丽日萱花照五云，升堂风采见乾淳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59067_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59067'>蓬莱会上逢王母，婺女光中见老人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59067_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59067'>雨露一门华发润，江山满座䌽衣新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59067_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59067'>只将千载苓为寿，更住人间九百春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59067_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59067'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59067_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年2月2日</a>　庐陵罗氏母百岁生日后一天，仍有诗赋之。作品：《拜罗氏百岁母之明日主人举酒客张千载心赋诗某喜赞不自已见之趁韵》<div id='poem_59165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59165?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拜罗氏百岁母之明日主人举酒客张千载心赋诗某喜赞不自已见之趁韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年2月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59165")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59165'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59165'>翠微三岛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>近，画阁五云横。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59165'>春水鸥声滑，夕阳鸦背明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59165'>尊前持一笑，花下卧馀酲<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作醒，据韩本、四库本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59165'>曾见瑶池母，不为虚此生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59165'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_59165'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_59165_0'>⑴ 原作鸟，据韩本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_59165_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年3月</a>　为王推官母写墓志铭。作品：《王推官母仇氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1320450' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320450' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320450?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王推官母仇氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320450")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320450_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320450'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320450'>东庐王先生母垂葬，命其门人文某铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320450_comment'></div>噫，某何以铭先生之母之墓哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320450_comment'></div>乃景定三祀，进士策御前，某以覆校待罪殿庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320450_comment'></div>一日，初考官第一卷拟上一览，某稍细复之，传观同官，惊讶得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320450_comment'></div>会一字近庙中嫌名，某以才难，白详定官请所以处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320450_comment'></div>临轩之日，赐出身，乃吾东庐先生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320450_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320450_comment'></div>使先生以名第取先天下，归拜母堂上，断机调熊，庶几夙昔，乃累先生以不释乎，此某其何以铭先生之母之墓哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320450_comment'></div>虽然，事孰为大，事亲为大，守孰为大，守身为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320450_comment'></div>使先生失身为亲忧，虽高科如之何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320450_comment'></div>先生虽不得高科，为臣忠，为子孝，身在焉，亲固荣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320450_comment'></div>谂先生曰然，铭无所辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320450_comment'></div>铭曰：母姓仇氏，世居庐陵之白沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320450_comment'></div>考讳彦诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320450_comment'></div>生二十二年，归于赠迪功郎致政君讳化权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320450_comment'></div>逮事姑两世，左右无违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320450_comment'></div>祭葬以礼，相夫子贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320450_comment'></div>调娱中和，靡失节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320450_comment'></div>子始就学，篝灯夜分，督厉吟讽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320450_comment'></div>及负笈从师，端以正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320450_comment'></div>手自纫缀，连寒暑弥不倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320450_comment'></div>以子入大学，甲寅明禋封孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320450_comment'></div>从子赴永州户曹，禄养寿康，称其命服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320450_comment'></div>咸淳七年三月十九日，终于家，年八十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320450_comment'></div>子二：长大琮，先孺人一年卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320450_comment'></div>次国望，从政郎、前袁州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320450_comment'></div>女四，一夭，二适李穆之，三适萧应祥，四适刘起岩，二与四先卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320450_comment'></div>孙六男，长渊，馀未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320450_comment'></div>五女，长适刘焕，次许彭麟，馀幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320450_comment'></div>九年三月壬申，厝于城西黄瘦山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320450_comment'></div>是为铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1320450_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年3月</a>　迁移先茔于山间。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年9月</a>　再次入京。吴潜再相，文天祥有贺文。作品：《贺吴丞相》<div id='poem_1320101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320101?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺吴丞相革启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320101")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320101'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320101'>再登铉路，首冠钧庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320101_comment'></div>以进士为名臣，两朝倚重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320101_comment'></div>以儒宗为宰相，四海具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320101_comment'></div>天启圣衷，国有生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320101_comment'></div>某官洪深而肃括，光大而直方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320101_comment'></div>乔岳泰山，微细悉归于涵育；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320101_comment'></div>青天白日，奴隶皆知其清明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320101_comment'></div>顷天子以为股肱，举海内望其风采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320101_comment'></div>霖雨未浃而收歛神功，泰阶未平而韬閟光耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320101_comment'></div>共惜温公之归洛，犹期潞国之还朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320101_comment'></div>偃逸藩维，久郁衮绣归公之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320101_comment'></div>均调鼎味，复端盐梅用汝之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320101_comment'></div>公卿大夫，交笏相庆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320101_comment'></div>儿童走卒，举手欢呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320101_comment'></div>顾中外不谋同辞，在今古未始多见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320101_comment'></div>斯人之望既切，贤者之责方新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320101_comment'></div>维今言路之不通，最为天下之大弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320101_comment'></div>缙绅以开口为讳事，城阙以游谈为危机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320101_comment'></div>如人一家，情睽离而众侮起；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320101_comment'></div>如人四体，气壅底而百病生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320101_comment'></div>多故之由，一类诸此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320101_comment'></div>枰更子改，柁转舟移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320101_comment'></div>惟从众谋，可以合天心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320101_comment'></div>惟广忠益，可以布公道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320101_comment'></div>尽解群疑众难之会，克有荣名成功之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320101_comment'></div>其惟我公，望在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320101_comment'></div>某瞻依有素，慕恋惟深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320101_comment'></div>适造阙以戒严，闻扬庭而增抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320101_comment'></div>以书上光范，先伸贺厦之私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320101_comment'></div>于人见欧阳，行展抠衣之敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320101_comment'></div>其为恳切，罔既敷宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320101_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1320101_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1259&endYear=1259')">1259年11月</a>　本年入京，逢董宋臣主张迁都，议论不下。文天祥即上疏一封，乞斩董宋臣，以安社稷。不报，还里。作品：《己未上皇帝书》<div id='poem_1319800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己未上皇帝书<span class='inlineComment2'>（开庆元年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1259年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319800")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319800'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319800'>十一月吉日，敕赐进士及第臣文天祥昧死百拜，谨奉诏献书于皇帝陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319800_comment'></div>臣一介疏贱，遭逢圣明，猥以庸愚，早膺亲擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319800_comment'></div>世道悠悠，风尘流靡，臣于其间盖尝感激奋发，以为由今之道，无变今之俗，一日有关于天下国家之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319800_comment'></div>惧以无辱使令，杜门四年，读《礼》之外，盖未尝一日不思以自效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319800_comment'></div>乃夏五，陛下临轩策士，偶垂记忆，起臣于家居，进臣于仕籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319800_comment'></div>臣伏被宸命，感激不自胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319800_comment'></div>追惟蒙恩之初，阻于朝谢，北望天路，辄奉表以闻，伏蒙圣慈许臣诣拜阙下，德至渥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319800_comment'></div>臣就道以来，不图国事浸艰，边烽顿迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319800_comment'></div>陛下引咎责躬，改过更始，召还旧德，斥去元奸，凡可以当天意回人心者，无所不用其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319800_comment'></div>伏惟陛下不自神圣，犹亲洒宸翰，诞布诏书，庶几中外臣庶危言极论，以有补于今日之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319800_comment'></div>陛下悔悟之意上通于天，天下于此感服陛下之勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319800_comment'></div>臣甫及趍谢阙庭，两读纶音，为之哽咽下泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319800_comment'></div>君臣之义，与天地并立，况臣蒙被厚恩，非众人比，使于此时泯泯默默，上负陛下，内负帝衷，尚何以饮食于载履间哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319800_comment'></div>是用不避斧钺，辄奋愚衷，条其说以献，惟陛下裁幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319800_comment'></div>一曰简文法以立事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319800_comment'></div>夫贵为天子，富有四海，垂衣拱手，以雍容于穆清之上，至尊之体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319800_comment'></div>不幸际时艰难，兵革四起，俯仰成败，呼吸变故，此非用马上治不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319800_comment'></div>今国势抢攘，固犹未至如马上之急，然寇入腹心，事干宗社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319800_comment'></div>陛下为皇皇拯救之谋，不得不略仿马上治之之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319800_comment'></div>今陛下焦劳于上，两府大臣黾勉于下，君臣之间，不可谓非日计军实而申儆之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319800_comment'></div>然尊卑阔绝，礼节繁多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319800_comment'></div>陛下平旦视朝，百官以次奉起居，宰相搢笏出奏，从容不踰时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319800_comment'></div>军国大事，此虽陛下日夜与宰相汲汲而图之，犹惧不既，谋王断国之设施，尊主庇民之蕴蓄，岂能以顷刻交际而究竟之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319800_comment'></div>陛下退食之暇，虽时出内批，以与宰相商论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319800_comment'></div>宰相又时有奏报，以出其建明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319800_comment'></div>然天下事得于面论者，利害常决于一言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319800_comment'></div>笔墨所书，或反覆数百言而不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319800_comment'></div>事机交投，寸阴可惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319800_comment'></div>使宰相常有此等酬酢，则一事之末，固有费其日力者矣，其于几务岂不有所妨哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319800_comment'></div>古者天子之于大臣，或赐坐，或赐食，或奏事至日昃，或论事至夜分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319800_comment'></div>凡皆以通上下之情，为国家至计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319800_comment'></div>赐茶之典，五代时犹有之，惟国初范质、王溥颇存形迹，此事遂废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319800_comment'></div>陛下莫若稍复古初，脱去边幅，于禁中择一去处，聚两府大臣，日与议军国大事，陛下赐之款密，亲是非可否于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319800_comment'></div>众议惟允，则三省画时施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319800_comment'></div>上下如一，都俞嘘咈之间，必将有超然度外之举，天下何事不可为，何难不可济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319800_comment'></div>至于除授，尤有关系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319800_comment'></div>且如近者重臣建阃之事，方帅海门，随迁建邺，甫镇建邺，又进上饶，布置变换，如弈棋然，卯诏辰行，奔命不给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319800_comment'></div>大者措画之如此，小者迁徙之更多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319800_comment'></div>人无定志，事无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1319800", 1319800, "Clauses/148/Comments/0")'>成谋</span>，当此艰危，岂不误事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319800_comment'></div>继自今始，陛下宜与大臣熟议，某人备某职，某人任某事，人物权衡，当而后用，朝廷命令，奠而后发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319800_comment'></div>如此，则观听者不至皇惑，驱驰者不至迟回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319800_comment'></div>人知其令出惟行，则无轻朝廷之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319800_comment'></div>士大夫知其可以展布四体，则鞠躬尽瘁而无观望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319800_comment'></div>其于国事，厥非小补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319800_comment'></div>又如用一人也，或出于陛下之拔擢，或出于宰相之启拟，中书已费行移，后省方及书读，或有不当，又至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1319800", 1319800, "Clauses/174/Comments/0")'>缴驳</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319800_comment'></div>比其不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1319800", 1319800, "Clauses/175/Comments/0")'>缴驳</span>也，则书黄径下，其人径受命矣，台谏始从而有所指陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1319800_comment'></div>是致国论纷纭，而内外职守迁移如传舍，施之平时，虽有体统，用之今日，恐误事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1319800_comment'></div>臣愚以为陛下宜仿唐谏官随宰相入閤故事，令给舍台谏从两府大臣日入禁中聚议。<div
