id='poem_sentence_26_1319802_comment'></div>惟皇上帝畀矜斯文，孔孟微言至我朝周、程、张、朱始大阐明，如朦斯发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319802_comment'></div>先皇帝表章四书，尊礼儒先，为往圣继绝学，为万世开太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319802_comment'></div>穆考之庙，称为理宗，陛下亲得精一之传，而日就月将，缉熙于光明，斯道斯民，解后千载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319802_comment'></div>先皇帝欲为唐虞三代之治，殆留与陛下使了此事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319802_comment'></div>臣睹陛下自践祚以来，畏天尊祖，亲亲仁民，敬大臣，体群臣，尊其所闻，行其所知，何往非学？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319802_comment'></div>今朝廷清明，宫府齐一，大法小廉，罔越厥志，不可谓不治矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319802_comment'></div>然臣切怪去年寒燠失常，四方或以旱告，今年星文示变，雨雹见妖，近者积阴为寒，皆名咎證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319802_comment'></div>汉人纵闭之学，必谓一證主事，臣不能晓此，但即其影而想其形，因其流而疑其源，岂人所不知，己所独知之也，陛下犹有当反之六经者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319802_comment'></div>陛下日御经筵，正道正言尝接于耳，而又内庭不废观书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319802_comment'></div>传曰「多识前言往行，以蓄其德」，陛下盖有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1319802_comment'></div>臣愚更愿陛下虚心体认，切己省察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1319802_comment'></div>每诵一义善，可以为法，即验之身，曰吾尝有是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1319802_comment'></div>无则勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1319802_comment'></div>每说一事恶，可以为监，即揣之心，曰吾尝有是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1319802_comment'></div>有则改之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1319802_comment'></div>言则虑其所终，行则稽其所敝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1319802_comment'></div>岂惟制治于未乱，保邦于未危，充道学之用，经纶天下之大经，范围天地之化而不过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1319802_comment'></div>行而帝，行而王，以卒先帝主张道统之事业，臣何幸身亲见之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1319802_comment'></div>《书》曰：「兢兢业业，一日二日万几」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1319802_comment'></div>夫一日二日之间，亦未至即有万事，然一事不谨，则万事之几，自此而兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1319802_comment'></div>故拨乱本，塞祸源，无一息不当用功，兢兢业业，所谓必有事焉者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1319802_comment'></div>惟陛下留神。</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1319802_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d6130f7f44334d3bb1199eab5797cab8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d6130f7f44334d3bb1199eab5797cab8");'><span id='d6130f7f44334d3bb1199eab5797cab8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年</a>，35岁</div><div id='d6130f7f44334d3bb1199eab5797cab8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年4月</a>　赴京走马上任，供监职，免兼右司。寻崇政殿说书，兼学士院权直等官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年</a>　上朝论对，有札子。作品：《轮对札子》<div id='poem_1319802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>轮对劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1268年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319802")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319802'>臣早以书生，遭遇先皇帝亲擢，事先皇帝垂十年，恨无涓埃补报天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319802_comment'></div>陛下龙飞继运，移忠以事圣明，永肩乃心，临鉴在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319802_comment'></div>比者臣来自外藩，待罪戎监，陛下亲御宸墨，进之经筵，臣学殖凋芜，循墙无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319802_comment'></div>自入侍毡厦，切见天颜睟穆，圣性谦虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319802_comment'></div>虽如草茅之愚，时赐访问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319802_comment'></div>臣感激殊遇，亦既得以悉数于前矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319802_comment'></div>猥当转对，伏念臣职在讲读，今日圣学关天下治忽不细，辄因封事，毕吐其衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319802_comment'></div>臣闻圣人之作经也，本以该天下无穷之理，而常足以拟天下无穷之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319802_comment'></div>天地无倪，阴阳无始，人情无极，世故无涯，千万世在后，圣人亦安能预窥逆观，事事而计之，物物而察之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319802_comment'></div>然后世兴衰治乱之故，往往皆六经之所已有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319802_comment'></div>凡六经垂监戒以为不可者，小犯之则关安危，大犯之则决存亡，如赴水火之必毙，如食堇葛之必毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319802_comment'></div>是何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319802_comment'></div>圣人知有理而已，合于理者昌，违于理者僵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319802_comment'></div>所贵乎帝王之学，惟能不悖乎六经，无蹈乎其大戒而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319802_comment'></div>呜呼，圣人所以为万世虑者岂不甚智，所以为万世戒者岂不甚仁矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319802_comment'></div>《书》曰：「民可近，不可下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319802_comment'></div>予视天下愚夫愚妇，一能胜予」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319802_comment'></div>而后世犹有以民为黔首，以覆其宗，为天下笑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319802_comment'></div>《书》曰：「内作色荒，外作禽荒」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319802_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「乱匪降自天，生自妇人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319802_comment'></div>而后世犹有昭阳、华清、霓裳羽衣，以阶渔阳之祸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319802_comment'></div>《书》曰：「谨乃俭德，惟怀永图」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319802_comment'></div>又曰：「不作无益害有益，不贵异物贱用物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319802_comment'></div>而后世犹有葡萄天马、甲帐翠被，以致四海萧然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319802_comment'></div>臣尝叹夫自圣经以来，时君不闻大道之要，生人不被至治之泽。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年7月</a>　入京除秘书少监、兼职依旧，遭台臣奏罢免，归里。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年</a>　归庐陵故居，有诗感怀。作品：《翰林权直罢归和朱约山韵》《用前人韵赋招隐》《借朱约山韵就贺挂冠》<div id='poem_59630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59630?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翰林权直罢归和朱约山韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1270年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59630")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59630_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59630'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59630'>闲云舒卷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_59630", 59630, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>无声画</span>，醉石敲推一色棋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59630'>试问挂瓢栖碧洞，何如襆被卧彤闱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59630'>梦中芳草还成路，别后黄花又是时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59630'>羞杀今年堂上燕，片心寄与雁南飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59630_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59630'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59630_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>借朱约山韵就贺挂冠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1270年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59512")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59512'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59512'>身健尚堪松下饭，眼明正好橘中棋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59512_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59512'>青山有约当朱户，白首何心上彩<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作粉）</span>闱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59512_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59512'>栗里田园供雅兴，午桥钟鼓赏清时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59512_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59512'>晚来倦客秋江上，坐看半天黄鹄飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59512_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59512'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59512_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='900f8234f56b43e08a9af613fe4287cf_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年</a>，40岁</div><div id='900f8234f56b43e08a9af613fe4287cf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年8月</a>　至临安阙下，驻兵西湖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月</a>　除浙西江东制置使、兼江西安抚大使、知平江府事。乞斩吕师孟，不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月16日</a>　除端明殿学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年9月27日</a>　辟周天骥、杨仔带、何时为参谋，从弟天祐分司徽州，林栋分司常州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年10月</a>　文璧弟旨除直秘阁，主管崇道观；二弟文璋充浙西制司内机。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='69bfef6823a44bc897fa301ae3ed9925_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("69bfef6823a44bc897fa301ae3ed9925");'><span id='69bfef6823a44bc897fa301ae3ed9925_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1276')">1275-1276年</a>，40-41岁</div><div id='69bfef6823a44bc897fa301ae3ed9925' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年12月</a>　召为签书枢密院事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年1月2日</a>　除临安府，辞不拜。指陈挽救社稷方略。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年1月13日</a>　劝丞相陈宜中不要会见元伯颜，不纳。接见义士杜浒，引为勤王力量。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　劝谏德祐皇帝，以陆秀夫奉益、广二王渡江出藩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年1月19日</a>　于临安早上除枢密使，午间除右丞相兼枢密使、都督诸路军马。以资政殿学士行元军营。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年1月</a>　抵达元营之情况，有诗记之。作品：《纪事》六首其一。《纪事》六首其二。《纪事》六首其三。《纪事》六首其四。《纪事》六首其五。《纪事》六首其六。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年1月</a>　抵达元营之情况，有诗记之。作品：《纪事》（狼心那顾歃铜盘）<div id='poem_58784' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58784' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58784?labeling=true' target='_blank'>纪事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_58784")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58784_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58784'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58784'>狼心那顾歃铜盘，舌在纵横击可汗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58784_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58784'>自分身为齑粉碎，虏中方作丈夫看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58784_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58784'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58784_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年1月21日</a>　宰相吴坚、贾余庆代表南宋政府投降。于是指责元伯颜失言，大骂吕文焕等人卖国。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年1月22日</a>　被羁留元营，斥骂元伯颜失信，申大义责骂吕文焕等诸降元贰臣。作品：《纪事》（不拼一死报封疆） 四首其一。<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗歌参《全宋诗》68册，第42990。）</span>《纪事》（虎头牌子织金裳） 四首其二。<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗歌参《全宋诗》68册，第42990。）</span>《纪事》（枭獍何堪共劝酬） 四首其三。<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗歌参《全宋诗》68册，第42990。）</span>《纪事》（麟笔严于首恶书） 四首其四。<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗歌参《全宋诗》68册，第42990。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年1月25日</a>　策罢所招义兵2万余，令各归其乡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年2月8日</a>　元军驱使文天祥随贾余庆等祈请使前往大都。随行北往诸客，唯留下杜浒及帐前将官八人。一路有诗记之颇多。作品：《使北》八首其一。<div id='poem_58849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>使北<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年2月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_58849")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58849'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58849'>自说家乡古相州，白麻风旨出狂酋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58849_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58849'>中书尽出降<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>元表，北渡黄河衣锦游<span class='inlineComment2'>（贾）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58849_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58849'></div><div id='poem_note_58849_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年2月</a>　元军驱使文天祥随贾余庆等祈请使前往大都。随行北往诸客，唯留下杜浒及帐前将官八人。一路有惊有险，以诗记之。作品：《闻鸡》《命里》《留远亭》二首其一。<div id='poem_59175' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59175' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59175?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻鸡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59175")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59175_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59175'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59175'>军中二十日，此夕始闻鸡。<div -----title
遂川
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2019c3260abf404293b4f0340307143a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2019c3260abf404293b4f0340307143a");'><span id='2019c3260abf404293b4f0340307143a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1261&endYear=1261')">1261年</a>，26岁</div><div id='2019c3260abf404293b4f0340307143a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1261&endYear=1261')">1261年</a>　春，游龙泉太霄观，有记。作品：《龙泉县太霄观梓潼祠记》<div id='poem_1320407' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320407' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320407?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙泉县太霄观梓潼祠记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1261年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320407")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320407_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320407'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320407'>龙泉邑治左，出门行数百步，有太霄老子宫焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320407_comment'></div>辛酉之春，予登其巅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320407_comment'></div>四山拱趍，天宇高旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320407_comment'></div>会令方营度作梓潼君祠，邀予为字曰「元皇之殿」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320407_comment'></div>既为从事，六月殿成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320407_comment'></div>明年，令若士以书谂曰：「役之初兴，君寔来，辱为之书，请卒记之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320407_comment'></div>邑为吉上游，山川清拔，民秀而文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320407_comment'></div>天圣以来，高科鼎鼎出，有位至侍从，以忠直自奋，尚论文献者归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320407_comment'></div>维郴实接壤，桴鼓数震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320407_comment'></div>令初至，适江上有警，郴寇益乘以噪，周旋军旅，不得以间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320407_comment'></div>事平，令谓：「吾幸为礼义邑，虽倥偬，不容不为俗化地，况少须暇乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320407_comment'></div>稽诸图志，庭庙鳞立，吾党之士，独无所敬祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320407_comment'></div>会宾兴诏下，乃进诸生谋曰：「今三岁大比，试者以文进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320407_comment'></div>将文而已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320407_comment'></div>意必有造命之神执其予夺于形声之表者，盖元皇是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320407_comment'></div>士之所自为，行为上，文次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320407_comment'></div>神所校壹是法，合此者陟，违此者黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320407_comment'></div>人谓选举之权属之有司，不知神之定之也久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320407_comment'></div>蜀山七曲神所宅之国，衣冠文物，莽为风尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320407_comment'></div>惟神元命，寔始吴会，英灵赫赫，将从君父所在而依之，是以江湖以南，神迹多著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320407_comment'></div>此固士之所当钦崇而景仰者，舍而不祠，惟缺典是惧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320407_comment'></div>议遂决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320407_comment'></div>予按《诗》曰：「相在尔室，尚不愧于屋漏」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320407_comment'></div>又曰：「昊天曰明，及尔出王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320407_comment'></div>昊天曰旦，及尔游衍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320407_comment'></div>夫人一动之微，必有神明焉，得其情于幽隐易肆之地，兹其所以体物而不可遗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320407_comment'></div>惟经传统谓之神，未有所指名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320407_comment'></div>近世贵进士科，士以得失为病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320407_comment'></div>自元皇庙食，于是始有司桂籍之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320407_comment'></div>化书所谓九十四化，变迁推移，旷千百岁，虽涉于不可测知，然神生为忠臣孝子，殁为天皇真人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320407_comment'></div>取士本末，实昉于人心义理之正，明有礼乐，幽有鬼神，果哉其不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320407_comment'></div>孟子曰：「天爵仁义忠信，人爵公卿大夫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320407_comment'></div>古之人脩其天爵，而人爵从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320407_comment'></div>圣贤不语怪，而教人先内后外，未尝非神之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320407_comment'></div>神虽游于太虚，而考德问业，初无戾于圣贤之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320407_comment'></div>其在祭法，苟有以明民成教，宜与祀典，则神之有祠，岂缁黄之宫之埒？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320407_comment'></div>邑有先民典刑，大冠逢掖，争志策厉，为臣止忠，为子止孝，此其内心固油然不自已，而况高山仰止，明神在前，则其戒谨恐惧，工力当倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320407_comment'></div>他日拔起诸生，彬彬知名，则居公卿大夫之位，必将有仁义忠信之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320407_comment'></div>令之此举，于人才甚有功，于方来世道非无所关系，岂曰以区区科目望其人，而惠徼福于神之一顾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320407_comment'></div>祠翼殿以庑，丹垩，具钟鼓供器如式，像设居中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320407_comment'></div>内而父母妇子事亲之道，孝之属也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320407_comment'></div>外而待御仆从为臣之道，忠之属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320407_comment'></div>费钱七十万有奇，十万为令俸，馀裒多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320407_comment'></div>迄于城观下，古曰「龙头里」，因其名为坊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1320407_comment'></div>扁额，校书郎姚君勉笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1320407_comment'></div>令方为远者计，廉用积馀，市田以奉祠事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1320407_comment'></div>继今邑之士，其受令之赐永永无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1320407_comment'></div>令陈氏，名升，三山人，初摄事，继辟今任云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1320407_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
高安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f69c46b3dba246bcaeda0c67cf14846e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f69c46b3dba246bcaeda0c67cf14846e");'><span id='f69c46b3dba246bcaeda0c67cf14846e_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年11月</a>　赴任瑞州。任上曾为诸学子讲说，以弘文教。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年12月</a>　本月迎亲慈就养。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　知瑞州。作品：《回衡州江判官启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作瑞州，据谭其骧地图改。）</span><div id='poem_1320257' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320257' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320257?labeling=true' "poem_title_1320257")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320257_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320257'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320257'>从军帷幄，欣云近于蓬莱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320257_comment'></div>赠我琼瑶，喜露承于霄汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320257_comment'></div>施先一介，礼后七襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320257_comment'></div>某官玉尺悬冰，金茎瀹露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320257_comment'></div>紫霄縻顶，扶摇溟海之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320257_comment'></div>绿水飘缨，谈笑郾城之月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320257_comment'></div>伫看飞鹗，即遂簉鸳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320257_comment'></div>某欣捧色丝，有华旧绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320257_comment'></div>撷潇湘之草，隃寄雁回；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320257_comment'></div>望江汉之云，莫将貂报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320257_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1320257_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1263&endYear=1263')">1263年</a>　知瑞州其间，因恩，天祥弟文璋奏名将仕郎，时年十七。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　在瑞州建野人庐、秀春亭、翠微亭、竹庵，创陶靖堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　本年有跋杨万里稿文。作品：《跋诚斋锦江文稿》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作瑞州，据谭其骧地图改。）</span><div id='poem_1320348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320348?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋诚斋锦江文藁<span class='inlineComment2'>（知瑞州日作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320348")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320348'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320348'>诚斋当淳熙之季，以少蓬出守，距今七十有七年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320348_comment'></div>某他日尝读《道院集》，见所品题甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320348_comment'></div>及来此，则先生一字之迹无复存者，惟亭阁尚留其名，而屋亦化为乌有矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320348_comment'></div>有则嵚㠌老压，亦未知其为当时屋否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320348_comment'></div>一日，得先生《锦江尺牍》一帙，大率吏楷，而为先生手笔者四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320348_comment'></div>其三盖在郡时作，其一作于还朝以后，而附诸帙尾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320348_comment'></div>典刑远矣，于此尚庶几见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320348_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320348_comment'></div>庚申一变，瑞之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1320348", 1320348, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>文物</span>煨烬十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320348_comment'></div>修复以来，得十年间残编断简，不啻足矣，而况出于七十年之前者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320348_comment'></div>且方其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1320348", 1320348, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>文物</span>具备之时，此帙非郡之所得有，收拾散亡之馀，乃能有前日之所未尝有，斯不谓之益奇矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320348_comment'></div>既勒诸石，书以识之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1320348_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年</a>　重修前守方逢辰未完之“三贤堂”并作记。作品：《瑞州三贤堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作瑞州，据谭其骧地图改。）</span><div id='poem_1320414' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320414' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320414?labeling=true' target='_blank'>瑞州三贤堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320414")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320414'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320414'>瑞有三贤祠堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320414_comment'></div>三贤：余襄公、苏文定公、杨文节公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320414_comment'></div>祠堂旧在水南阛阓，景定庚午燬于兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320414_comment'></div>前守严陵方君逢辰迁之稍西，垂成而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320414_comment'></div>某为君代，相遇于上饶，君语及斯堂，曰：「瑞人之敬三贤也如生，三年无所于祠，意闵闵焉，予是以亟新之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320414_comment'></div>然涂塈未毕，像设未备，子其成之，成则为之记」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320414_comment'></div>某至郡，既敬奉君之教，遂率诸生行释菜礼，而君书三至，谂记之成，某不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320414_comment'></div>夫瑞为郡，号「江西道院」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320414_comment'></div>然在汴京盛时，为远小，故余、苏二公皆以谪至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320414_comment'></div>淳熙间，郡去今行在所为近，而杨公江西人，虽自蓬监出守，殊不薄淮阳也，地一而时不同，又守郡者与他谪异，然瑞人矜而相语，槩曰：「吾郡以三贤重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320414_comment'></div>余公坐党范文正；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320414_comment'></div>苏公坐救其兄东坡先生，后又以执政坐元祐党；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320414_comment'></div>杨公坐争张魏公配享事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320414_comment'></div>使此三贤者皆无所坐，安得辱临吾土」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320414_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320414_comment'></div>甚矣，瑞人之好是懿德也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320414_comment'></div>然三贤所养，犹有可得而窃窥者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320414_comment'></div>范公忤吕丞相而去也，未几复用，前日夤缘被斥者以次召还；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320414_comment'></div>襄公自瑞徙泰，乃独请岭南便郡以归，愈去愈远，岂非所谓同其退不同其进者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320414_comment'></div>苏公世味素薄，其记东轩，谓颜氏箪瓢之乐不可庶几，而日与郡家收缁铢之利，曾不以为屈辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320414_comment'></div>异时再谪，三徙之馀，退老颍滨，杜门却扫，不怨不尤，使人之意也消。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320414_comment'></div>若杨公，则肆意吟哦，笔墨淋漓，在郡自为一集，与畴昔道山群贤文字之乐无以异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320414_comment'></div>若三贤者，岂以摈斥疏远累其心哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320414_comment'></div>夫摈斥疏远不以累其心者，其流或至于翛然远举，超世遗俗，而三贤又不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320414_comment'></div>余公用于庆历，苏公用于元祐，蹇蹇匪躬，皆在困踬流落之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320414_comment'></div>杨公当权奸用事，屡召不起，报国丹心，竟以忧死，凛然古人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1320414", 1320414, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>尸谏</span>之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320414_comment'></div>呜呼，此其所以为三贤欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320414_comment'></div>繇前言之，吾知在瑞之时，乐天安土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320414_comment'></div>繇后言之，吾知在瑞之时，乃心罔不在王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320414_comment'></div>呜呼，此其所以为三贤欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320414_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「高山仰止，景行行止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320414_comment'></div>太史公曰：「虽为之执鞭，所欣慕焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320414_comment'></div>瑞人之敬三贤也，又于此思之，当有以称方君所为欲记斯堂之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320414_comment'></div>某于先正，无能为役。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1320414_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年9月</a>　修复碧落堂，重阳与客赋诗。作品：《题碧落堂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作瑞州，据谭其骧地图改。）</span><div id='poem_59278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题碧落堂<span class='inlineComment2'>（知瑞州日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1264年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59278")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59278'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59278'>大厦新成燕雀欢，与君聊此共清闲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59278'>地居一郡楼台上，人在半空烟雨间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59278'>修复尽还今宇宙，感伤犹记旧江山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59278'>近来又报秋风紧，颇觉忧时鬓欲斑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59278'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59278_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年10月</a>　应诏赴京，除礼部郎官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1264&endYear=1264')">1264年11月</a>　除江西提刑，辞免不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年2月</a>　在瑞州交割提刑职事。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泰和
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6770590829c5467f9c0dfa4130379d73_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6770590829c5467f9c0dfa4130379d73");'><span id='6770590829c5467f9c0dfa4130379d73_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年</a>，30岁</div><div id='6770590829c5467f9c0dfa4130379d73' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1265&endYear=1265')">1265年4月</a>　伯祖母梁夫人殁，申解官承心制。遭黄万石论罢。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bd2fe21069eb4c3a80a6771588ba5dfa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bd2fe21069eb4c3a80a6771588ba5dfa");'><span id='bd2fe21069eb4c3a80a6771588ba5dfa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>，44岁</div><div id='bd2fe21069eb4c3a80a6771588ba5dfa' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>由南安军经行赣州、吉州途中，有诗记之。作品：《泰和》<div id='poem_59206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59206?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泰和</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59206")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59206'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59206'>书生曾拥碧油幢，耻与群儿共竖降。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59206'>汉节几回登快阁，楚囚今度过澄江。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59206'>丹心不改君臣谊，清泪难忘父母邦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59206'>惟有<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作恐）</span>乡人知我瘦，下帷绝粒坐蓬窗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59206'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过泰和，作诗祭悼友人袁德亨。作品：《悼袁德亨》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗存《泰和钟步袁氏族谱》）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宣城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ffd731f6487e4dd7b76c51f3c80b3ffb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ffd731f6487e4dd7b76c51f3c80b3ffb");'><span id='ffd731f6487e4dd7b76c51f3c80b3ffb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1270')">1269-1270年</a>，34-35岁</div><div id='ffd731f6487e4dd7b76c51f3c80b3ffb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1269&endYear=1269')">1269年</a>　上任宁国府事。作品：《回江州李都承与书》《回潘检阅书》《回钟编校尧俞书》《与游提刑汶书》《与赵知郡孟荻书》《与赵监丞淇书》<div id='poem_1319993' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319993' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319993?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回潘检阅书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319993")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319993_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319993'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319993'>某伏以岁华晼晚，春事权舆，共惟某官镂玉晶荧，凝旒简注，神之相之，台候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319993_comment'></div>某浓熏鹊尾，酬敬腆施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319993_comment'></div>曩从集英殿门，吾榜得人，以执事重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319993_comment'></div>海台沙合，云月相辉，至今斗牛犹有光气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319993_comment'></div>顾山林僻左，系雁悠悠，天际碧云，明发不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319993_comment'></div>千里眉目，忽照宛陵，为之跫然以喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319993_comment'></div>钦以某官歛昆崙以为神气，捲溟渤以为波涛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319993_comment'></div>玉质金相，宛乎无自眩之色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319993_comment'></div>泉清松茂，浩然有难进之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319993_comment'></div>乃今䌷石室之秘藏，为籀书而出色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319993_comment'></div>视周六典，作宋一经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319993_comment'></div>南丰以史学称，进裁大典；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319993_comment'></div>安定非他人比，宜在经筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319993_comment'></div>某鹤梦正臞，起废出坎，循墙弗获，被命于征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319993_comment'></div>郡枵然虚，真山凋水瘵处也，敏手爬梳，犹惧不蔇，况不颖之尤者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319993_comment'></div>不规而颂，非所敢望于同年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319993_comment'></div>禀酬崖经，宁不嗣音？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319993_comment'></div>愿言努力明德，对扬王休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319993_comment'></div>有昭亭委戒，其敢不肃！</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1319993_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1319994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回钟编校尧俞书<span class='inlineComment2'>（字君俞，号方岩。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319994")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319994'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319994'>某晓汲冻清，以贽万一之谢，首干穹勺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319994_comment'></div>某两年山中，风月晃朗，望太乙光气九霄，吾书无翰，不能时一飞到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319994_comment'></div>梅花月影，忽疑是君，而米家第二帖至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319994_comment'></div>施稠报眇，自省欿如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319994_comment'></div>尊执事以黼黻云汉之胸，试金玉典坟之手，驾轻就重，拾级升高，此逢掖之至荣，而搢缙之交羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319994_comment'></div>曾子固晋裁大典，为史学优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319994_comment'></div>胡康侯宜在经筵，非他人比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319994_comment'></div>某鹤梦正寒，大化驱之出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319994_comment'></div>自湖涉江，风帆回薄，四十程乃抵宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319994_comment'></div>山凋水瘵，眇兮愁予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319994_comment'></div>敏手爬梳，犹惧不蔇，况不颖之尤者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319994_comment'></div>高明局外之见，何以教之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319994_comment'></div>满砚冰澌，濡毫如帚，尚规嗣音，以写缱绻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1319994_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1319998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与游提刑汶书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319998")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319998'>某以良月之望，举棹东下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319998_comment'></div>江空见底，乃章贡源头，诸水怒长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319998_comment'></div>未几，光燄五朵，与空同云俱来，往帆顺风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319998_comment'></div>航波澜之澎湃，洒石钟之清越，宠灵张王，迄抵双溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319998_comment'></div>子月丙寅，俯祗贱役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319998_comment'></div>瓣香西望，敬谢所蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319998_comment'></div>明公卷其十二峰之神气，轩轩磊磊，照耀东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319998_comment'></div>以宰相才，学宰相事，天下久望其为家毡出色，辔丝周道，肯复倭迟？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319998_comment'></div>惠露瀼瀼，江之民幸矣，如溥寰何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319998_comment'></div>会有温纶，四辈驰下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319998_comment'></div>某不善为斲，得郡复枵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319998_comment'></div>至之日，视官官靡，视吏吏荒，民气愦愦如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319998_comment'></div>爬剔棼丝，顾气力所至，终觉五技易穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319998_comment'></div>肘后神奇，不敢以望之他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319998_comment'></div>惟故山松菊，衣被䌽云，亦已过数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319998_comment'></div>矧兹陇蜀，徼惠未涯，微畴昔不及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319998_comment'></div>相望二千里外明月，此心恳恳，侧釐挂一漏万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319998_comment'></div>惟青阳时动，绨绿光华，式金式玉，以副前祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319998_comment'></div>此岂无骪，辱戒为荣。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1319998'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1319998_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1319999' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319999' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319999?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与赵知郡孟荻书<span class='inlineComment2'>（号菊山）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319999")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319999_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319999'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319999'>某顷从南浦亭边，抖擞殷函，道所蒙荷，且矫首于太乙之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319999_comment'></div>穹林冥坐，缥缈绛霄，江涂漫漫，劳我宵栩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319999_comment'></div>执事以玉雪界之精神，临睨八极，朝阆风，夕玄圃，识者犹窃迟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319999_comment'></div>锦衣照道，紫淦横舟，荡漾柳风，嘘吸竹露，涧阿乐矣，如颙颙望岁者何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319999_comment'></div>建章夜半，尺一堂堂，画省红云，著公高处，惟日望之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319999_comment'></div>某不善为斲，得郡复枵，以子月丙寅视篆昭亭下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319999_comment'></div>视官官靡，视吏吏荒，洗垢爬痒，亦曰视吾气力所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319999_comment'></div>然山凋水瘵，非刀圭可疗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319999_comment'></div>肘后神奇，惠徼大福，某不敢以望他人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319999_comment'></div>焚蕤瀹雪，西乡奉书，以谢以祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319999_comment'></div>鼎珍履絇，愿言金护玉持，对扬王休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319999_comment'></div>临风悁结。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1319999_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1320001' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320001' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320001?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与赵监丞淇书<span class='inlineComment2'>（号平远）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1269年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320001")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320001_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320001'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320001'>某乃岁之秋，缇骑来山中，岳翠苍寒，琳琅照映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320001_comment'></div>章不成报，内有欿然，宁不嗣音，僻左之以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320001_comment'></div>世道如许，风起云飞，中夜人物之思，为此耿耿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320001_comment'></div>上念井络，丹诏起家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320001_comment'></div>峡月栈云，先声浩荡，盖有望木牛流马，再立武侯之事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320001_comment'></div>又壁窥万一，意必与南山洎予秀诸公上下云龙，共此光明俊伟之举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320001_comment'></div>缩手袖间，临睨天半，此其大本领、大经纶，政不易涯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320001_comment'></div>野水横舟，苍虬缥缈，山君川后，日有疏附，即日恭惟台候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320001_comment'></div>某渔隈半席，自分小休，误渥自天，俾寻庾、谢旧盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320001_comment'></div>意此是抆拭笭箵之陋耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320001_comment'></div>三辟弗可，乃以阳月之望，束书出山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320001_comment'></div>涉重湖，越大江，整整四十日抵戍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320001_comment'></div>以是月丙寅祗贱事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320001_comment'></div>凋城败屋，枵然大瓠耳，搔首踟蹰，望洋气缩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320001_comment'></div>维宣距邺，仅隔一云，东望熏香，奉尺书候起处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320001_comment'></div>惠徼药石，立我沈痼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320001_comment'></div>梅花晴昊，拄笏神驰。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1320001'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1320001_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年1月1日</a>　本月初一，除军器监兼右司，辞免不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年1月</a>　江万里本月二十九离都赴洞霄宫，天祥有别诗。作品：《临岐饯别》<div id='poem_59462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临岐饯别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1270年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59462")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59462'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59462'>圣恩优许力求田，把酒临岐饯一杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59462'>台阁是非远已矣，乾坤俯仰愧何哉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59462'>竟追范蠡归湖去，不管胡儿放马来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59462'>强圉倘殷如孔棘，也应定策救时危<span class='inlineComment2'>（清雍正十二年《江氏宗谱》）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59462'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1270&endYear=1270')">1270年3月</a>　交待宁国府有关职事，准备履新。<br /></div>

-----title
衡阳（衡州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1b1ec72b236a4bbbaa57b22222bdd266_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1b1ec72b236a4bbbaa57b22222bdd266");'><span id='1b1ec72b236a4bbbaa57b22222bdd266_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>，38岁</div><div id='1b1ec72b236a4bbbaa57b22222bdd266' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年5月1日</a>　本月初一，抵达衡阳，受印，领职事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年5月</a>　友人邹仲翔忽病死，为之撰写墓志铭。作品：《邹仲翔墓志铭》<div id='poem_1320447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320447' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320447?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邹仲翔墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320447")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320447_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320447'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320447'>景定五年，予奉亲高安，除提点江西刑狱，谢弗拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320447_comment'></div>适寇起兴国之东，庐陵犬牙相错，所在骚动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320447_comment'></div>余所居乡，一鬨千室，大家以去为望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320447_comment'></div>邹君仲翔，中人之金也，率乡人栅东门山为备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320447_comment'></div>山下阻衣带水，君恐仓卒涉者为鱼，架浮梁以济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320447_comment'></div>明年春，寇一日蓐食行三百里，薄太和之王山，距余乡半舍而近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320447_comment'></div>乡人扶携老稚走险，微一不善脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320447_comment'></div>君经纪山寨，当是时，一乡之命悬于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320447_comment'></div>讫寇去，君保护无有害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320447_comment'></div>时余<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1320447", 1320447, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>避节</span>弗获命，会枢密督以捕逐，文移旁午，余以乡部嫌，将重以请，慨然曰：「奈何以我辞受，坐视龙蛇为赤子困乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320447_comment'></div>于是即日受印，下令会兵，诸山寨皆署长，君与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320447_comment'></div>未几，寇平，余罢归里，于溪之上游，斩荆莽，燔椔翳，得奇观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320447_comment'></div>君欣然从予山中，匹马一童，朝至而暮忘归，率以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320447_comment'></div>余每集宾从，君辄在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320447_comment'></div>闻余语中理解，未尝不解颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320447_comment'></div>间从余言：「人生何为碌碌，弃家事从公游，可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320447_comment'></div>余谢非余所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320447_comment'></div>君曰：「吾意决矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320447_comment'></div>乃尽以伏腊属其子，而颓然以休，访予南北厓某水某丘，若将终身焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320447_comment'></div>癸酉夏四月，余行湘，君送余于香城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320447_comment'></div>后一月，君以疾死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320447_comment'></div>余闻之，欷歔不自禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320447_comment'></div>湘之归也，未及门，望见其子来，哽不能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320447_comment'></div>呜呼，余岂私君！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320447_comment'></div>君与人必以情，闻义辄赴，见有不善，面折不少回，而不藏怒，不宿怨，旷如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320447_comment'></div>君虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1320447", 1320447, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>赤手起家</span>，而好施出其性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320447_comment'></div>岁饥，发粟给其比邻二百户，能捐殖以自损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320447_comment'></div>道太和甃十里，道庐陵甃六十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320447_comment'></div>衣寒者，食饥者，病者馈药，死者予棺，丧无归者葬其土，度其能为，辄不少吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320447_comment'></div>君之族前有长者，以善植门为益国周文忠公所知，去之百年，风流相接焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320447_comment'></div>余尝谓君慈而乐舍，大率浮屠家所尚，至临难急病，能御灾捍患，以有德于乡闾，大夫士或愧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320447_comment'></div>君名凤，仲翔其字，世为富川人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320447_comment'></div>曾祖大明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320447_comment'></div>祖人杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320447_comment'></div>考世兴，妣梁氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320447_comment'></div>娶萧氏、梁氏，皆先卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320447_comment'></div>子男一人，曰成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320447_comment'></div>女三人，适郭镠、王镕、刘锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320447_comment'></div>孙男二人，梦龙、复生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320447_comment'></div>君得年六十有四，以甲戌十一月某日葬于其乡沙洲平之原，治命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320447_comment'></div>君之先人，尝卜地于东门山之下，曰：「吾父葬于是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320447_comment'></div>溯山而上为龙头，得一丘焉，曰：「吾藏骨焉，吾后其兴乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320447_comment'></div>君晚而优游，有子治生，有孙业于学，咸以为验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320447_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1320447'>东门之原，君之父兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1320447_comment'></div>东门之麓，君之母兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1320447_comment'></div>东门之巅，君所构兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1320447_comment'></div>瞻彼东门，相尔后兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1320447_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年5月</a>　居衡阳公所，有谢皇帝表。作品：《湖南提刑到任谢皇帝表》<div id='poem_1319806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖南提刑到任谢皇帝表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319806")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319806'>帝庭敷命，昭辟四门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319806_comment'></div>天牧播刑，误颁一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319806_comment'></div>申以遄驱之旨，畴兹已试之庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319806_comment'></div>周隰载驰，汉条具布<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319806_comment'></div>伏念臣本无他技，惟有孤忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319806_comment'></div>两朝特达之知，荐尘清要；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319806_comment'></div>十载行藏之迹，秪自悔尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319806_comment'></div>云雷之义方屯，天地之心已复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319806_comment'></div>当元日达聪之始，在皇华遣使之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319806_comment'></div>圣恩靡许于祝釐，臣职敢稽于行道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319806_comment'></div>瞻盖高而下耳，冀用誉于折肱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319806_comment'></div>兹盖恭遇皇帝陛下道协重华，仁周四表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319806_comment'></div>崇德广业，合乾转坤翕之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319806_comment'></div>折狱致刑，得震动离明之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319806_comment'></div>遂令承乏，复忝司平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319806_comment'></div>臣敢不祗若咨询，对扬钦恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319806_comment'></div>陈时臬事，尚弘康乂之图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319806_comment'></div>受王嘉师，永迪明清之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319806_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1319806_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4066762b5e9b4836a631444f42360265_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4066762b5e9b4836a631444f42360265");'><span id='4066762b5e9b4836a631444f42360265_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1274')">1273-1274年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='4066762b5e9b4836a631444f42360265' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年11月</a>　道州太守徐宗斗在讨寇中以身殉职，为之写墓志铭。作品：《祭道州徐守宗斗文》<div id='poem_1320460' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320460' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320460?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭道州徐守宗斗文<span class='inlineComment2'>（温州人，文武两科。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320460")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320460_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320460'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320460'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320460_comment'></div>龙虎变化兮人物之英，风霆流行兮宇宙之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320460_comment'></div>天下之啬兮一州之赢，三年而一日兮侯度是程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320460_comment'></div>及召驿之垂驾兮，胡疢之婴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320460_comment'></div>没而可食于南邦兮，忧民忧国之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320460_comment'></div>某交谊兮云仍，王事兮弟兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320460_comment'></div>乐莫乐兮知心，悲莫悲兮余哭之茕茕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320460_comment'></div>下神与兮临蒸，桂棹兮积雪斲冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320460_comment'></div>操弧矢兮上征；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320460_comment'></div>绝虎虺兮纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320460_comment'></div>噫至人兮无死，歆余奠兮如生。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1320460_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年11月</a>　友人刘定伯卒，为之撰墓志铭。作品：《刘定伯墓志铭》<div id='poem_1320449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘定伯墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320449")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320449'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320449'>余东家诗人刘君定伯，类晋宋间旷达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320449_comment'></div>自余辟山水南北崖落，然不可人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320449_comment'></div>君时从予招，或不约径造，至则善为言谭，名理蜂出，意所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1320449", 1320449, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>左右</span>，辩者不可诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320449_comment'></div>江山朝暮四时之变，嘲咏赏啸，兴出物外，常使人讽念不可忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320449_comment'></div>嗜奕，最入幽眇，兔起鹘落，目不停瞬，解剥摧击，其势如风雨不可御，胜败不落一笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320449_comment'></div>饮酒可一二斗，酒酣浩歌，声振林木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320449_comment'></div>或投冠袒裼，旁若无人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320449_comment'></div>或鼻息雷鸣，径卧坐上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320449_comment'></div>君豪纵，沛然以为自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320449_comment'></div>当其乐时，不知天之高，地之下，老之将至焉尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320449_comment'></div>予前在宣州，君以诗来，思致<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1320449", 1320449, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>清迈</span>，恨不即投印绶，从君烟霞之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320449_comment'></div>既归，君好日以怡，诗日以张大，于是盖年五十三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320449_comment'></div>乃孟夏一日过予，极论当世事，抑扬不少挫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320449_comment'></div>诘旦报曰，君<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1320449", 1320449, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>痰厥</span>逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320449_comment'></div>予骇亟视之，不复可为，哭失声狂，三日不能止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320449_comment'></div>非予为然，凡与君交者，谈君辄挥涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320449_comment'></div>里之人不问倪旄，叹伤如出一口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320449_comment'></div>噫，可人在天地间，鬼神所忌邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320449_comment'></div>君长身五尺馀，坚壮耐寒暑，须发如漆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320449_comment'></div>性落魄，不问家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320449_comment'></div>家才三四口，粗了伏腊，不为求赢，有钱辄不惜鸡黍，送客无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320449_comment'></div>朋友<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1320449", 1320449, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>有无相通</span>，急难于我乎赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320449_comment'></div>平生于人无诺责，乡人有为芥蒂，君一语辄化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320449_comment'></div>有不善，开譬之，无以为望，和气薰浃，蒸然<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1320449", 1320449, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>善邻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320449_comment'></div>一岁半为四方客，主君者所至投辖，惟恐亟去，虽儿童仆厮无不诚爱君者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320449_comment'></div>君破崖岸，削边幅，不为拘拘孑孑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320449_comment'></div>至道理所在，确然守之不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320449_comment'></div>其执丧为孝子，按丧礼，门内不入缁黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320449_comment'></div>一子二侄，命以先畴瓜分而三，无赢缩薄厚，子曰敢不共命，侄曰敢固辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320449_comment'></div>一家兴仁兴逊，乡曲相传为盛门，非好德畴至是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320449_comment'></div>君始祖邽，长沙人，为吉州长史，家于西昌之九洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320449_comment'></div>四世祖德远徙庐陵富川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320449_comment'></div>君之三世曰文焕、子玉、邦贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320449_comment'></div>妣邹氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320449_comment'></div>娶张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320449_comment'></div>子男梓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320449_comment'></div>女淑容，适彭天麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320449_comment'></div>卜以次年咸淳癸酉十一月壬辰，封于淳化乡扶竹坑枫树塘之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320449_comment'></div>君名澄，定伯字也，自号前村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320449_comment'></div>有诗集，自编，曰《前村初稿》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320449_comment'></div>君诗不为深苦，而清拔雄健，如其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320449_comment'></div>有子能力学，不坠义方，君死何憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320449_comment'></div>予所憾者，君死独何蚤，泣而为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320449_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1320449'>其坚也骤折，其劲也蚤摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1320449_comment'></div>命之臧凶，匪系其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1320449_comment'></div>生也达，死也何怛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1320449_comment'></div>君墓我铭，我心则结。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1320449_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年11月4日</a>　冬至日，撰贺冬启，遣使专送。作品：《贺前人冬启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（具体时间由录者推算。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年</a>　冬，为更好照顾母亲家人，请求量移至故里附近赣州守。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年1月</a>　为贺新年，奉札江相，有贺启；后寻春回，互送春酒，又有回启。作品：《贺前人正启》《回前人送春启》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年1月15日</a>　州人贺元宵佳节，有感而撰文纪念。作品：《衡州上元记》《齐天乐·甲戌湘宪种德堂灯屏》（夜来早得东风信）<div id='poem_1320421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衡州上元记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320421")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320421'>岁正月十五，衡州张灯火，合乐，宴宪若仓于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320421_comment'></div>州之士女倾城来观，或累数舍，竭蹶而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320421_comment'></div>凡公府供张所在，听其往来，一无所禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320421_comment'></div>盖习俗然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320421_comment'></div>咸淳十年，吏部宋侯主是州，予适忝陈臬事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320421_comment'></div>常平以王事诣长沙，会改除，于是侯与予为客主礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320421_comment'></div>是晚，予从城南竟城东，夹道观者如堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320421_comment'></div>入州，从者殆不得行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320421_comment'></div>既就席，左右楹及阶，阶及门，骈肩累足，𧥄𧥄如鱼头，其声如风雨潮汐，咫尺音吐不相辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320421_comment'></div>侑者集三面之人，趋而前，执事几不可曲折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320421_comment'></div>酒五行，升车诣东厅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320421_comment'></div>厅之后稍偏，为燕坐，俎豆设焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320421_comment'></div>主人既肃宾，车不得御，乃步入燕坐之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320421_comment'></div>至，儿童妇女杂袭而争先，男子冠以上往往引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320421_comment'></div>及献酬，州民为百戏之舞，击鼓吹笛，斓斑而前，或蒙倛焉，极其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1320421", 1320421, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>俚野</span>，以为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320421_comment'></div>游者益自外至，不可复次序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320421_comment'></div>妇女有老而秃者，有羸无齿者，有伛偻而相携者，冠者，髽者，有盛涂泽者，有无饰者，有携儿者，有负在手者，有任在肩者，或哺乳者，有睡者，有睡且苏者，有啼者，有啼不止者，有为儿弁髦者，有为总角者，有解后叙契阔者，有自相笑语者，有甲笑乙者，有倾堂笑者，有无所睹随人笑者，跛者，倚者，走者，趋者，相牵者，相扶擎者，以力相拒触者，有醉者，有勌者，咳者，唾者，嚏者，欠伸者，汗且扇者，有正簪珥者，有整冠者，有理裳结袜者，有履阈者，有倚屏者，有攀槛者，有执烛跂惟恐堕者，有酒半去者，有方来者，有至席彻者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320421_comment'></div>儿童有各随其亲且长者，有无所随而自至者，立者，半坐于地者，有半坐杌下者，有环客主者，有坐复立者，有立复坐者，视妇女之数，多寡相当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320421_comment'></div>盖自数月之孩以至七八十之老，靡不有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320421_comment'></div>其望于燕坐之门外，趑趣而不及近者，又不知其几千计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320421_comment'></div>当是时，舞者如傩之奔，狂之呼，不知其亵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320421_comment'></div>观者如立通都大衢，与俳优上下，不知其肆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320421_comment'></div>予与侯颓然其间，如为家人之长，坐于堂，而骄儿騃女充斥其间，不知其偪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320421_comment'></div>予起而举酒祝侯曰：「以平易近民，而民近之，岂弟父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320421_comment'></div>侯之谓矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320421_comment'></div>侯酬且执爵前曰：「惟使者使民不冤，无湮郁其和，我是以大有民」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320421_comment'></div>予避且谢，则复诸侯曰：「使时和岁丰，日星明概，举海内得以安其生而乐其时，衡与赐焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320421_comment'></div>维天子之功，臣等何力之有」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320421_comment'></div>侯拱而立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320421_comment'></div>侯，蜀人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320421_comment'></div>因与予言益州承平时，元夕宴游，其风流所亲见，盖出于祖宗德泽，天地涵育之久，而今不可复得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320421_comment'></div>予悯然私念之，开庆、景定间，衡以中州，不得免于难，今城郭室庐，公私文物，犹草创绵蕝云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320421_comment'></div>然以几世几年所为郡，而十数年间卒然脩复，得其大体，非国家忠厚积累，于民力爱养有素，岂望如今所成立哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320421_comment'></div>蜀自秦以来，更千馀年，无大兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320421_comment'></div>至于本朝，侈繁钜丽，遂甲于天下，不幸荡析，若鬼神之忌盈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320421_comment'></div>今衡之民务本而勤力，岁时一观游之外，衣食其耕桑，俭而不泰，风气淳厚，犹南方建德之国，其将进而未已者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320421_comment'></div>予为亲怀归，得郡且行，侯选表于朝有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320421_comment'></div>惟一时民物之槩，得于目击，相与嗟叹，阔绝而欣喜，不厌于心者，不当无所纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320421_comment'></div>且惧夫可爱可愕之状，俯仰蹉跌，忽不可以复追也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320421_comment'></div>燕之明日，亟奋笔记之，以庶几观风之意，且使后来者于侯政有考焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320421_comment'></div>侯名遇，今居延平。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1320421'></div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1320421_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>齐天乐<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>甲戌湘宪种德堂灯屏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320139_comment'></div>春风渭北之旗，夜月洞庭之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320139_comment'></div>箫韶俗耳，冰雪征尘。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320141_comment'></div>飞卷五云之风雨，光华九日之山川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320141_comment'></div>味也冞深，恩斯曷称。<div class='inline' "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319920")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319920'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319920'>某干犯师严，辄有申请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319920_comment'></div>秦寇之在广西，扰动二十五郡，为梗累年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319920_comment'></div>去年破贺之富川，官民荼毒不细，经司不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319920_comment'></div>今破我永明，杀死知县，杀伤县尉、主学，捲去县印，屠居民，掳妇女，掠去财物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319920_comment'></div>继而又破永明之下泽，又寇我江华，移其所以毒广西者施之湖南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319920_comment'></div>此而不讨，失刑莫大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319920_comment'></div>广西以前独力不能捕灭，今何幸湖南肯与会合，宿兵以待师期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319920_comment'></div>朝廷之主张方新，言路之指陈甚力，此扫清巢穴之一机，为两路官民舒泄冤愤，不可失之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319920_comment'></div>前经帅不足望，满望新经帅之来，不料意见参差，施行矛盾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319920_comment'></div>兹得经司牒报，捕贼以官，授贼以职，犒贼以酒，赏贼以钱，凡怀忠愤，无不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1319920", 1319920, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>弹指</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319920_comment'></div>自昔化贼为民，固有称为盛德事者，盖贼有出于田里之饥荒，激于官吏之贪黩，弄兵之情，出不获已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319920_comment'></div>故仁人处之，念其为赤子，姑惟安之，勿庸胜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319920_comment'></div>今秦寇招募无徒，建置将校，横行两路，啸聚千群，戕天子之命吏，劫公府之铸印，杀人盈野，罪如丘山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319920_comment'></div>既非胁从，又非乌合，渠魁纵有求降之说，官司亦在不受之科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319920_comment'></div>而况初无出首之真情，仅取改过之文状，谩曰回乡而安业，何曾束身以归官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319920_comment'></div>得之广人所云，一面受招，一面劫杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319920_comment'></div>刑政无章，宜其至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319920_comment'></div>天下之大势相维，所仗者义而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319920_comment'></div>若名义不著，大之不可以立国，小之不可以立家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319920_comment'></div>今观广西，成何宇宙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319920_comment'></div>先生不忍斯人之涂炭，一再调兵，必欲罪人斯得然后已，此真扶持人极，纲维世变，盛心之所推也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1319920_comment'></div>但今来广西既作此可笑举措，未必不以龚遂渤海之事自诡，上惑圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1319920_comment'></div>本路冒然进兵，非惟蹊径不熟，乏隅总乡导之助，有悔吝之虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1319920_comment'></div>亦恐邻阃反以本路为张皇，坏其儿戏之前功，或者阴设陷阱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1319920_comment'></div>今直须申审朝省，看指挥如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1319920_comment'></div>朝旨主招谕，本路只得撤兵，后有冲突，广西当任其咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1319920_comment'></div>朝旨如以招谕为不然，自是督两路会合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1319920_comment'></div>至时湖南不求广西，而广西自当约湖南共事，此利害自是坦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1319920_comment'></div>谨具公申，欲望备申朝省，仍乞钧翰与当揆商订，必须计一例断行下，曰招则招，曰捕则捕，使人无中立之疑，则亦无事后之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1319920_comment'></div>所有永明县见驻劄，有使阃之兵，有本州之兵，有谢隅官之义丁，约近千人，日费舂陵供亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1319920_comment'></div>比来徐守已费支吾，郡力凋薄，亦为可念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1319920_comment'></div>今高节所部兵若到山前，不过又是坐食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1319920_comment'></div>愚意谓不若候朝旨行下，确许讨捕，然后调往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1319920_comment'></div>今乞且唤回高节一行军兵归营，听候朝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1319920_comment'></div>某非敢违使阃约束，本司去山前颇近，的见利害如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1319920_comment'></div>恃师门相与之真，故敢倾臆以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1319920_comment'></div>拱听处分，以凭遵守。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1319920_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1273&endYear=1273')">1273年10月27日</a>　十月乙亥，江万里生日。有贺诗。作品：《寿古心江先生》<span class='inlineComment2'>（本诗《全宋诗》似不见。）</span><div id='poem_59348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59348?labeling=true' target='_blank'>古心江先生以旧弼出镇长沙癸酉十月乙亥是为七十六岁门人文某以一节趋走部内谨拟古体一首为寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1273年10月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59348")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59348'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59348'>炎图启丕运，皇路熙以平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59348'>蜿蟺发令姿，有美洵一人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59348'>鸿藻舒朝华，大音锵韶钧。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59348'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_59348", 59348, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>黼珽</span>丽三阶，火龙昭紞纮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59348'>桓圭殿南服，熊旂被金城。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59348'>瞻彼鹑为火，翼轸宣其精。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59348'>祥鸾舞瑶席，鸣凤翔娲笙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59348'>孟冬兆阳气，西北无浮云。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59348'>驾言酌春酒，可以写我情。<div id='poem_sentence_8_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59348'>扬旌下祝融，躧履朝泰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>清。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59348'>嘉猷扇九垓，还以邃古淳。<div id='poem_sentence_10_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59348'>君子保金石，所以永国成。<div id='poem_sentence_11_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_59348'>纯嘏锡千岁，绵绵赞休明。<div id='poem_sentence_12_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_59348'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_59348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_59348'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_59348_0'>⑴ -----title
赣州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5c7e6aab3c99436b9610865e80278b86_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5c7e6aab3c99436b9610865e80278b86");'><span id='5c7e6aab3c99436b9610865e80278b86_link'
