href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年3月2日</a>　转任赣州，初二抵达。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年</a>　到达赣州后，即上谢表。作品：《知赣州到任谢皇帝表》<div id='poem_1319818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319818' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319818?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知赣州到任谢皇帝表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319818")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319818_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319818'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319818'>九重选牧，锡类天宽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319818_comment'></div>千里承流，奉亲地近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319818_comment'></div>昉共侯度，丕戴王休<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319818_comment'></div>伏念臣某才本空疏，分安孤苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319818_comment'></div>身逢盛代，夙自厉于丹心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319818_comment'></div>家有重亲，晚相依于白发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319818_comment'></div>顷叨汉传，往即楚封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319818_comment'></div>何敬非刑，粗殚审克；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319818_comment'></div>不遑将母，私切怀归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319818_comment'></div>尝恳恳以陈情，冀高高之欲从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1319818_comment'></div>遄蒙异渥，特畀近麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1319818_comment'></div>继朌旨以趣征，已鞠躬而祗上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1319818_comment'></div>禄及一门之微贱，恩同大造之生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1319818_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下以尧舜之资，行曾闵之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1319818_comment'></div>嗣宁王之大历，毖我成功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1319818_comment'></div>奉太后之万年，与天齐寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1319818_comment'></div>遂使忝求刍之寄，亦获共啜菽之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1319818_comment'></div>臣敢不老老及人，亲亲为政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1319818_comment'></div>由家达国，期兴逊以兴仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1319818_comment'></div>以子移臣，寓为忠于为孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1319818_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1319818_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年4月</a>　在赣州，专函拜候江万里。作品：《通潭州安抚大使江丞相书》<div id='poem_1319935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1319935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1319935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通潭州安抚大使江丞相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1261年10月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1319935")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1319935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1319935'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1319935'>某在门墙诸孙辈行中，而所以蒙钧天造就，知爱绸缪，独出乎诸生之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1319935_comment'></div>然号为登门垂二十年，而至今庭下无愈之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1319935_comment'></div>古人负笈从师，不间道路之远，某乃不能自拔如此，殆不可对人言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1319935_comment'></div>兹者诚不自意先生手提王钺，作镇于重湖以南，而某适以臬事一节，奔走于赐履之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1319935_comment'></div>昔者詹企台阶，坐霄壤隔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1319935_comment'></div>今乃得以诣大府，受约束，有一日歛板之便，岂天殆为小子计乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1319935_comment'></div>某始以亲老丐祠，即趣旨下，再请则渎，于是姑以单车出门，盖驰驱数旬，又须乞便郡归养耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1319935_comment'></div>某四月八日辞膝下，留庐陵城中，始闻先生拜乾会节于清江，亟亟追逐，牙纛度宜春、醴陵间，所蹉跌片云间耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1319935_comment'></div>兹专布状，重谢不敏，且致恭先之悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1319935_comment'></div>参谒迩只，溯风距踊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1319935_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年4月</a>　在赣州任上，再次复函江万里。作品：《与前人时以前宰相帅湖南回启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（今《全宋文》本似不存。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年6月</a>　六月，庆祝祖母刘夫人八十七寿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年10月</a>　在赣州 ，撰有行状、记文多篇。作品：《雷州重建醮楼记》《雷州十贤堂记》《知潮州寺丞东岩先生洪公行状》<div id='poem_1320423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雷州重建谯楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320423")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320423'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320423'>凡并海而为州，皆有飓风，而雷为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320423_comment'></div>中州多山，地气固密，城郭公府，苟非水火兵革之难，虽累数千百年，存焉可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320423_comment'></div>南方岁有飓风，拔大木，蜚大屋，以为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320423_comment'></div>矧雷三面际海，当风之冲，岂独城楼难哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320423_comment'></div>太史氏虞侯应龙来为守，是为咸淳十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320423_comment'></div>六月十有二日夜半，飓风作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320423_comment'></div>厥明，视谯压而城坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320423_comment'></div>方风之来也，其晕如虹，有蜃气如楼台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320423_comment'></div>及其歘霍凌轹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1320423", 1320423, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>訇哮</span>撞搪，其声不可名状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320423_comment'></div>侯曰：「斯楼，郡以昼夜者，非大且壮，无以支永久」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320423_comment'></div>乃筏钜材，鸠工并兴，设为巍峨，下临鲸波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320423_comment'></div>人闻而怃然曰：「天下犹海也，世变犹风也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320423_comment'></div>昔人有言：大厦非一木可支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320423_comment'></div>又曰：震风凌雨，而后知厦屋之帡幪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320423_comment'></div>侯所建立，有安天下之道焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320423_comment'></div>侯之为雷也，宽而有制，严不为暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320423_comment'></div>始至，蒐军明律，戮泽中为龙蛇者，狱有三年淹破其货内者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320423_comment'></div>覈丁籍，实民赋，老壮以时，富贫有经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320423_comment'></div>又为之表贤哲，兴学校，开其伦常，示人有耻，陶为清淳，讼是用希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320423_comment'></div>凡此皆侯所为反风徙鳄之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320423_comment'></div>天子圣神文武，克有天命，祝融受职，海若顺令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320423_comment'></div>侯为政知所本，价人维藩，式是南邦，城楼云乎哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1320423_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1320422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雷州十贤堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320422")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320422'>国朝自天禧、乾兴迄建炎、绍兴，百五十年间，君子小人消长之故，凡三大节目，于雷州无不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320422_comment'></div>按雷《志》、丞相寇公准以司户至，丁谓以崖州司户至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320422_comment'></div>绍圣后，端明翰林学士苏公轼、正言任公伯雨以渡海至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320422_comment'></div>门下侍郎苏公辙以散官至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320422_comment'></div>苏门下正字秦公观至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320422_comment'></div>枢密王公岩叟虽未尝至，而追授别驾，犹至也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320422_comment'></div>未几，章惇亦至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320422_comment'></div>其后丞相李公纲，丞相赵公鼎，参政李公光，枢密院编脩官胡公铨，皆由是之琼，之万，之儋，之崖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320422_comment'></div>正邪一胜一负，世道以之为轩轾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320422_comment'></div>雷视中州为远且小，而世道之会乃于是观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320422_comment'></div>我度皇之九年，诏太府寺簿虞侯应龙知雷州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320422_comment'></div>侯，雍公曾孙，有文学，凡登朝必与史事，诸所衮钺得《春秋》大旨，植之风声，尚有典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320422_comment'></div>其至雷也，考图谍，访耆老，顾瞻山川，惄如有怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320422_comment'></div>乃黜丁氏、章氏，自莱公以至澹庵凡十贤，为祠于西湖之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320422_comment'></div>使海邦兴起前闻，一朝皂白，知所以劝，敬贤如师，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1320422", 1320422, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>疾恶如仇</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320422_comment'></div>侯所为岂刀笔细故哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320422_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320422_comment'></div>雷何地也，诸贤冠冕于此，俨然而威，自太守诸生以下，敬恭登降，制币荐奠如先圣先师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320422_comment'></div>人有常言，「惟是风马牛不相及也」，诸贤何以得此于南海，南海何以得此于诸贤乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320422_comment'></div>我祖宗待士大夫忠厚而有礼，稽诸司败，岭海则止，此事上配帝王，非汉唐所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320422_comment'></div>虽施之奸回，容有伤惠，而贤者失路，靡不获全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320422_comment'></div>祈天永命，万有斯年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320422_comment'></div>噫嘻，盛德事也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320422_comment'></div>祠经始于十年九月，十月吉日落成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320422_comment'></div>侯谓予同馆，走书数千里至赣，属予记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320422_comment'></div>予不敏，叙其凡，复为迎送神辞，使祀则歌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320422_comment'></div>辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1320422'>飙风起兮云黄，万里兮故乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320422_comment'></div>桃茢兮祓不祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320422_comment'></div>何怀乎斯宇兮，惟独有此众芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320422_comment'></div>海可竭兮神不可忘，五岳为质兮三辰为光，保我有国兮万年其昌。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1320422_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1320441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知潮州寺丞东岩先生洪公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320441")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320441'>东岩先生洪公，盖阳岩先生文毅公族诸弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320441_comment'></div>文毅公以孤忠遗直著闻当世，其平生言论风旨，讲切上下，公未尝不在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320441_comment'></div>文毅公屡召不赴，公浸向用，辄落落不合去，时论称为二洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320441_comment'></div>文毅公既没，泉南文献之望尽属公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320441_comment'></div>识者谓文毅公未为者，将有为也，而公又不及大用以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320441_comment'></div>天之生才，倏忽代谢，安得不深慨于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320441_comment'></div>叙次行事，谂诸方来，门人之责，奚以辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320441_comment'></div>公讳天骥，宇逸仲，自号东岩，世晋江县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320441_comment'></div>嘉定戊辰七月庚戌，公以生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320441_comment'></div>生有异质，沈静专一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320441_comment'></div>自少讲求微言，通念晓析乃已，故于经史诸子百家之辞无不贯串，文章自成一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320441_comment'></div>以绍定改元荐于乡，名声振一时，学子蹐门，愿求模楷者日众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320441_comment'></div>公坦明夷粹，专以宿于道为教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320441_comment'></div>逮事王大母，一夕疾甚殆，公不解带，不交睫，至剔股肉杂汤药进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320441_comment'></div>公一念之切通于神明，然终身不以语人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320441_comment'></div>登淳祐七年进士第，初筮邵武军建宁县尉，发擿奸伏，当官无所回挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320441_comment'></div>时有劫寇王若曾，啸聚千馀人，骚动两路，诸所委捕多畏沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320441_comment'></div>公奋不顾身，提兵捣其巢，一举空之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320441_comment'></div>伪造成风，为楮币蠹，公密设方略，动中肯綮，李若聂凡三大党与，无不各就缚，文献之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320441_comment'></div>石壁胡公颖、秋崖方公岳交章以公善状闻于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320441_comment'></div>十二年，循从政郎，调连州推官，未上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320441_comment'></div>宝祐改元，旨差监惠民南局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320441_comment'></div>四年，较艺南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320441_comment'></div>公考镜详密，精力不间昼夕，所赏拔士多根柢理致，当时号明有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320441_comment'></div>公虽浸近周行，然无所附丽，恂恂侃侃，望之山立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320441_comment'></div>徐公清叟、吴公燧、马公光祖、颜公颐仲俱剡上其能，将用矣，会有言者，徒步西归，泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320441_comment'></div>六年，淮阃择士，自从首辟，致公为属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320441_comment'></div>景定二年，通班授宣教郎、知广州香山县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320441_comment'></div>至之日，以教养人才为第一义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320441_comment'></div>脩复大成殿，明伦有堂，主敬美身宾贤登俊有斋，皆捐俸入为之，歛不及民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320441_comment'></div>其为政一裁于义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320441_comment'></div>俗哗健，戢其尤桀黠者，曰：「此囚牙讼师去，则吾民妥矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320441_comment'></div>邑以大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320441_comment'></div>洪公勋、赵公汝暨、雷公宜中及仓宪交以邑最上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320441_comment'></div>咸淳元年，转奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320441_comment'></div>二年，差监行在榷货务都都茶场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320441_comment'></div>四年，吴公革、冯公梦得、赵公顺孙、刘公黻皆以吏才为荐，差监都进奏院，转朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320441_comment'></div>冯公时为刑侍，及户侍刘公应龙交委以书，拟本部文字，公皆乐为知己尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320441_comment'></div>于时上即位逾年，初政新美，公轮当陛对，宿斋豫戒，冀积忱意悟上心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320441_comment'></div>取虞廷君臣时几之说寓规焉，其一曰君心勤怠之几，二曰人心离合之几，三曰君子小人消长之几，四曰中国外夷强弱之几，及朱文公天理人欲之辨，首尾二千馀言，其辞谆复恳切，深刺腧髓，玉音叹美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320441_comment'></div>又言，泉有屯戍左翼一军乏兴之害，米舟搜籴生变之虞，而朝廷籍没翁、林二氏之田，可岁得谷万斛，以纾戍卒两月廪食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320441_comment'></div>或有不济，寺院及单丁住持，令本州覈实区处，并拨为军饷之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320441_comment'></div>饷足则籴宽，籴宽则米通，民永无贵籴患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320441_comment'></div>朝论翕然，以为论事有阳岩风，除大理寺簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1320441_comment'></div>五年，转朝散郎、知潮州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1320441_comment'></div>公之在潮也，视民事如家，视<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1320441", 1320441, "Clauses/155/Comments/0")'>敝政</span>如己疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1320441_comment'></div>捐金以裕学廪，倾囷以粟饥民，梁川以利病涉，知无不为，为无不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1320441_comment'></div>潮与漳、汀接壤，盐寇畲民群聚剽劫，累政以州兵单弱，山径多蹊，不能讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1320441_comment'></div>公应变设奇，降者相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1320441_comment'></div>又欲于接境置屯，多者三百人，少者二百人，掎角为援，郡为创撙节库以赡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1320441_comment'></div>具有条画，悉以言于朝，并下之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1320441_comment'></div>漳、汀放此，且严保伍之令，以澄其源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1320441_comment'></div>大抵公智虑深达如宿将，持重而规画绵络，不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1320441", 1320441, "Clauses/181/Comments/0")'>以邻为壑</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1320441_comment'></div>又潮有护田旧堤，多齧于水，貤俸与民，筑石为堤，民号之曰洪公堤，且刻赋颂其旁，曰：「此我公东岩生佛所为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1320441_comment'></div>去之日，垂髫戴白者拥车下不忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1320441_comment'></div>公雅意林壑，至是则曰：「吾可优游，乐吾真矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1320441_comment'></div>九年，得旨主管华州云台观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1320441_comment'></div>公时益畅于诗，数与姻族觞咏从容，而学徒有志于考德问业者，多授以外声利及终身受用之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1320441_comment'></div>暇日登临徜徉，爱南安之间风气明秀，取所谓小陂山者曰：「乐哉斯丘，我死则葬焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1320441_comment'></div>预饬美槚，治寿藏，澹然尘外蝉蜕之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1320441_comment'></div>十年正月，公始属微疾，即乞以本官生前致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1320441_comment'></div>八日，忽索水自浴衣冠，休于正寝，翛然而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1320441_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1320441_comment'></div>若公者可谓启手足而不乱，其风流笃厚真足以追配文毅公于九原而无怍者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1320441_comment'></div>某于公之门，实丙辰省屋诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1320441_comment'></div>戊辰之春，待罪中朝，谂日拜公床下矣，未及而去国，然于公之践脩出处之槩，盖心识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1320441_comment'></div>共惟穆陵丰芑菁莪之泽，涵育天下，天下士猬然勃兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1320441_comment'></div>温陵邈在海隅，人物相望，阳岩之气节焕发乎其前，东岩之抱负翼承乎其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1320441_comment'></div>使二公诚得尽展拓，又未知孰后孰前也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1320441_comment'></div>呜呼，今复见斯人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1320441_comment'></div>曾祖遇，妣陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1320441_comment'></div>祖德明，妣李。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1320441_comment'></div>父伯道，赠宣教郎，妣陈，赠安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1320441_comment'></div>元妃陈，先二十六年卒，赠安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1320441_comment'></div>继赵，封安人，先三年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1320441_comment'></div>子男应午、应申、应寿，俱业进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1320441_comment'></div>女四，适胡登龙、丘公赐、王毓奇，一尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1320441_comment'></div>应午力学克肖，收拾公遗稿若干卷，曰《东岩集》，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1320441_comment'></div>将以是年十月己未，奉治命以葬，赵安人附殡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1320441_comment'></div>应午千里贻书，俾某状行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1320441_comment'></div>姑序其本末，以俟立言之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1320441_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_81_1320441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年</a>　弟文璧改办浙西安抚司，升制置主营机宜文字司存。改制置两浙主营官告院，仍旧职举最。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1274&endYear=1274')">1274年</a>　赣州任上，撰有多篇诗赋文章。作品：《题郁孤台》《予题郁孤泉管五湖翁姚濂为之和翁官满归里因韵贽别并谢前辱》《翠玉楼晚雨》《翠玉楼观雪》《翠玉楼和胡端逸韵》《翠玉楼》《合江楼二首》《皂盖楼》《石楼》《马祖岩》《禅关》《吸江》《尘外》《云端》《清江何汉英再见于空同读欧阳先生诗感慨为赋》《送曹倅岩山官满归里》《邹文叔垂芳堂记》《封孺人罗母墓志铭》《乐庵老人刘氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_59619' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59619' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59619?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郁孤台</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59619")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div id='poem_sentence_0_59619_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59619'>并天浮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_59619", 59619, class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59544'>采芝云满山，采檗瀑垂涧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59544'>当年有清徽，为寄南来雁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59544'>雁去人已逝，岁月剨云晏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59544'>流水失声音，西河老忧患。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59544'>往日志士悲，穷途行子惯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59544'>君为梁宋游，我复江汉宦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59544'>十年耿相逢，千里欠一盼。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59544'>玄机寄糟粕，美疢堕刍豢。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59544'>赠子归东方，聊荐吴兴苋。<div id='poem_sentence_8_59544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59544'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_59544_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59173' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59173' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59173?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送曹倅岩山官满归里<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59173")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59173_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_59173_0'>① 名大（原作夫，据四库本改）发，赣倅</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59173'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59173'>春陵光霁落苍苔，葛水神仙立翠槐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59173'>万里云霞麒骥路，三年风月凤凰台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59173'>兴同老子复不浅，歌曰先生归去来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59173'>庾岭梅花开渐遍，一枝就与寄蓬莱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59173_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59173'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59173_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1320409' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320409' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320409?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邹文叔垂芳堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320409")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320409'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320409'>吾乡上游，有佳木连理，生于邹公长者之地，不知几何年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320409_comment'></div>益公取以补《庐陵图志》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320409_comment'></div>木滨水如老蛟，夭矫有腾骧怒起之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320409_comment'></div>咸淳八年秋，一夕大雷电以风，木随水而飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320409_comment'></div>又二年秋，有莲一蒂双华，出于文叔北窗下苔池中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320409_comment'></div>文叔，长者曾孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320409_comment'></div>连理表章于乾淳间，邹氏始享有其瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320409_comment'></div>予闻长者一再传，皆恂恂友爱，同气并根，既硕且蕃，实生来仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320409_comment'></div>今文叔之庭，二季竞爽，两孙端美，天将昌之，其殆视同颖两岐絪缊坱圠而未有已乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320409_comment'></div>文叔喜而命予题其堂，曰「垂芳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320409_comment'></div>夫一草一木之微，比于太虚，仅同毛发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320409_comment'></div>而「鄂不韡韡，兄弟之亲」，《小雅》所为赋也，于吾心得无感乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320409_comment'></div>予旦夕尚徘徊新堂，为君赓《棠棣》之一章。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1320409_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1320445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>封孺人罗母墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320445")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320445'>乃咸淳九年，庐陵融斋居士罗氏生母满百岁，融斋之夫人时年七十六，白发在堂，事百岁母如妇礼，子孙孙子环侍起居，为男女三十有奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320445_comment'></div>予乡称庆门，必曰新安罗氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320445_comment'></div>其年二月朔，予从里中士奉币载酒，拜百岁母堂上，母答拜，诸孙皆拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320445_comment'></div>饮母，母釂酢宾，诸孙各执爵从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320445_comment'></div>既成礼，夫人视予年家子，不听去，为之留三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320445_comment'></div>为诗以歌其事，好事者或为图以传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320445_comment'></div>国家承平，休养生息，用康于人，眉寿无有害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320445_comment'></div>传曰：「礼水有芑，数世之仁也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320445_comment'></div>夏，予将指于湘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320445_comment'></div>未数月，闻夫人讣，欷歔失声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320445_comment'></div>问百岁母安乎，曰：「安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320445_comment'></div>母于今盖百踰一矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320445_comment'></div>夫人将葬，其孤以是母命来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320445_comment'></div>予后母生六十三年，得载笔承命铭夫人，自昔能言所未有，乃叙次其凡系之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320445_comment'></div>夫人姓萧氏，吉水人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320445_comment'></div>曾祖琢，祖曾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320445_comment'></div>父异，乡贡进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320445_comment'></div>妣廖氏，继张氏、徐氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320445_comment'></div>归承务郎致仕士友，是为融斋居士，先七年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320445_comment'></div>子男五：浚，先五年卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320445_comment'></div>煜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320445_comment'></div>植；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320445_comment'></div>耕，脩职郎、前监行在奉口酒库；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320445_comment'></div>垕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320445_comment'></div>女一，适儒林郎侍班周寿申，先二十九年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320445_comment'></div>孙男九，寀、寯、宦、寔、寓、宜、绍、颢、平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320445_comment'></div>女十一，长适张栋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320445_comment'></div>曾孙男七，举孙、颖孙、元孙、满孙、怡孙、真孙、复孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320445_comment'></div>女二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320445_comment'></div>夫人以庚申明禋恩封孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320445_comment'></div>卒之年七月十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320445_comment'></div>次年十二月某日，封于所居里柘径之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320445_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1320445'>昔唐夫人之为崔母兮，逮事长孙皇姑兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320445_comment'></div>姑年高齿落以枯兮，升堂乳之劬劬兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320445_comment'></div>姑曰妇恩之不可孤兮，愿世世子孙之不渝兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320445_comment'></div>夫人五世崔如兮，母年踰百崔所无兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320445_comment'></div>胡不与寿为徒兮，为此母怃兮，为夫人吁兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1320445_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1320448' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320448' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320448?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐庵老人刘氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1274年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320448")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320448_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320448'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320448'>余读《汉陆贾传》，甚羡余邻翁乐庵刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320448_comment'></div>贾择田地，家好畤，出橐中千金，析其五男，安车过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320448_comment'></div>数击鲜，十日而更，以寿终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320448_comment'></div>余尝谓人生晚福优游，宜莫如贾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320448_comment'></div>当是时，韩、彭俎醢，酂侯周勃犹不免械系，求为贾一日，得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320448_comment'></div>翁生四子，皆有才智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320448_comment'></div>四十年即弃家政，就养诸子，以次第循环，五日一更，其设馔务为相高，惟恐不得其欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320448_comment'></div>翁饥来得食，渴来得饮，早眠晏起，一切不顾人间事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320448_comment'></div>惟时时接方外士，讲铅汞之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320448_comment'></div>间取松柏，惟意咀啖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320448_comment'></div>翁年过七十，而颜色如童，摄生有助焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320448_comment'></div>或谓陆生作《新语》，为汉达官，非翁匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320448_comment'></div>余曰不然，贾艰难嬴、项间，从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1320448", 1320448, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>马上公</span>为客，一再使越，崎岖万里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320448_comment'></div>翁生于世，长于世，老于世，不出乡，终其天年，有乐于其身，无忧于其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320448_comment'></div>设贾复生，校翁失得，未必以彼易此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320448_comment'></div>翁又有数事异甚，里传鬼车鸣者，未夜相戒，灭明，屏息户内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320448_comment'></div>翁开楼大呼，愿见鬼车，卒无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320448_comment'></div>有神以祸福惊人，翁过其祠，持牛炙如常，人莫不危恐，翁休休如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320448_comment'></div>尝有所营造，忌某星直某方，翁曰：「犯者殆乎，请身当之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320448_comment'></div>某星迄不验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320448_comment'></div>为子简妇，或云妇不利于长，翁不为夺，自是诸昏嫁历家说格不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320448_comment'></div>中年卧疾，家人私召女巫，谋为厌胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320448_comment'></div>翁廉知之，强起逐之出门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320448_comment'></div>未属纩，翁默自念作其像赞，若辞而远游者，顾左右曰：「吾死，勿事缁黄，吾志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320448_comment'></div>医以药进，麾使去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320448_comment'></div>问日入乎，曰然，反面而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320448_comment'></div>江南之俗尚鬼，其人畏死而信巫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320448_comment'></div>翁能自不惑，非由耳传口授，殆一至之性然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320448_comment'></div>翁名邦美，字才卿，乐庵其自号也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320448_comment'></div>始祖邽，长沙人，为吉州刺史，家西昌九洲，后徙庐陵富川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320448_comment'></div>三世曰德远、文焕、子玉，妣曾氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320448_comment'></div>娶陈氏，先三十七年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320448_comment'></div>继祁氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320448_comment'></div>其子孙实蕃，济生机，洪生桂、槐、植、模，深生朴、柚，乡贡进士浩生枢、楫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320448_comment'></div>槐复生癸孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320448_comment'></div>女二，适于梦牛、曹雷应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320448_comment'></div>孙女五，适邹、曹，许曹、罗，一幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320448_comment'></div>翁八岁丧母，十六岁丧父，移其事父母事兄长终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320448_comment'></div>岁时上丘冢拜祖祢，率诸后生，尚有典刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320448_comment'></div>翁富寿安逸，推其一念孝友，殆命物所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320448_comment'></div>诸孙方将以诗书大其门，翁必为人宗乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320448_comment'></div>翁生庆元戊午二月庚午，殁咸淳癸酉正月丙辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320448_comment'></div>后二年正月，葬于淳化乡凫塘之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320448_comment'></div>余家距翁一垣，翁年吾祖之下，吾父之上，谂翁有年数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1320448_comment'></div>深与余游且厚，来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1320448_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1320448'>其生也有涯，其死也有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1320448_comment'></div>尔世其昌，匪我铭其谁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1320448_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1275&endYear=1275')">1275年1月13日</a>　接获勤王诏书，遂召集诸路豪杰数万众，奉诏勤王，欲入卫临安。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4f022e73729a40a083462831d34cd201_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4f022e73729a40a083462831d34cd201");'><span id='4f022e73729a40a083462831d34cd201_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>，44岁</div><div id='4f022e73729a40a083462831d34cd201' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年5月28日</a>　本日随元军解舟至赣州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年5月</a>　由南安军经行赣州、吉州途中，有诗记之。作品：《黄金市》<div id='poem_59236' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59236' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59236?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄金市</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59236")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59236_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59236'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59236'>闭蓬绝粒始南州，我过青山欲首丘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59236'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_59236", 59236, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>巡远</span>应无儿女态，夷齐肯作稻粱谋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59236'>人间早见黄金市，天上犹迟白玉楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59236'>先子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_59236", 59236, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>神游</span>今二纪，梦中挥泪溅松楸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59236'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59236_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

衢州
-----detail

苏州

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3月3日</a>　是夜出真州逃，三更抵达扬州西门，不敢入，从者四人逃。作品：《出真州》十三首其一。《至扬州》二十首之一。<div id='poem_58741' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_0_58741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58741'>谁知关出西门外，憔悴世间无告人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58741_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3月4日</a>　流亡藏匿于扬州城西，几乎被数万元军发现。作品：《至扬州二十首》之十一。<div id='poem_58800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_58800")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58800'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58800'>此庙何神三十郎，问郎行客忒<span class='link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3月5日</a>　行藏在扬州贾家庄败墙粪秽中。是夜，走高邮，失道。作品：《贾家庄》<div id='poem_59220' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59220' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a -----title
高邮

id='poem_sentence_1_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59534'>夜行二百里，望望无人烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59534'>迷途呼不应，如在盘中旋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59534'>昏雾腥且湿，怒飙狂欲颠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59534'>流澌在须发，尘沫满櫜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>鞬。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59534'>红日高十丈，方辨山与川。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59534'>胡行疾如鬼，忽在林之巅。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59534'>谁家苦竹园，其叶青<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_10_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59534'>绕林势奔轶，动地声喧阗。<div id='poem_sentence_11_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_59534'>霜蹄破丛翳，出入相贯穿。<div id='poem_sentence_12_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_59534'>既无遁形术，又非缩地仙。<div id='poem_sentence_13_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_59534'>猛虎驱群羊，兔鱼落蹄筌。<div id='poem_sentence_14_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_59534'>一吏射中目，颈血仅可溅。<div id='poem_sentence_15_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_59534'>一隶缚上马，无路脱纠缠。<div id='poem_sentence_16_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_59534'>一厮躏其足，吞声以自全。<div id='poem_sentence_17_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_59534'>游锋几及肤，怒兴空握拳。<div id='poem_sentence_22_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_59534'>跬步偶不见，残息忽复延。<div id='poem_sentence_23_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_59534'>当其蹙迫时，大风起四边。<div id='poem_sentence_71_59534'>圣世基岱岳，皇风扇垓埏。<div id='poem_sentence_71_59534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_59534'>中兴奋王业，日月光重宣。<div -----title
泰州（海陵）

id='poem_sentence_1_59107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59107'>出<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>路相传险，行囊愈觉悭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59107'>归心风絮乱，无柰一身闲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59107'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_59107'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_59107_0'>⑴ 韩本、四库本作去</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_59107_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_58754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>发海陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_58754")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58754'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58754'>自海陵来向海安，分明如渡鬼门关。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58754'>若将九折回车看，倦鸟何年可得还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58754_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58754'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58754_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南通（通州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5bc83afbcc67465cac631f1fa1186c87_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5bc83afbcc67465cac631f1fa1186c87");'><span id='5bc83afbcc67465cac631f1fa1186c87_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　由海陵，过海安、如皋，于本日至通州。一路有诗感怀记之。作品：《闻马》《如皋》《闻谍》《怀扬通州》<div id='poem_58890' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58890' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_58890")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58890_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58890'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58890'>过海安来柰若何，舟人去后马临河。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58890_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58890'>若非神物扶忠直，世上未应侥倖多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58890_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58890'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58890_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58769' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58769' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58769?labeling=true' "poem_title_58769")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58769_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58769'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58769'>雄狐假虎之林皋，河水腥风接海涛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58769_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58769'>行客不知身世险，一窗春梦送轻舠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58891'>不是神明扶正直，淮头何处可安身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58891'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58891_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>怀扬通州<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_58833")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58833'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58833'>江波无柰暮云阴，一片朝宗只此心。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58833'>今日海头觅船去，始知百炼是精金。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58833_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58833'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58833_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58836?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58836'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58836'>唤渡江沙眼欲枯，羁臣中道落崎岖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58836'>乘船不管千金购，渔父真成大丈夫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58836_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58836'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58836_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58834?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58834'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58834'>范叔西来变姓名，绨袍曾感故人情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58834'>而今未识春风面，倾盖江湖话一生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58834'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58834_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58835?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58835'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58835'>仲连义不帝西秦，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_58835", 58835, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>拔宅</span>逃来住海滨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58835'>我亦东寻烟雾去，扶桑影里看金轮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58835_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58835'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3闰</a>　在通州，给《指南录》撰写序言。作品：《指南录·自序》<div id='poem_1320328' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320328' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320328?labeling=true' target='_blank'>指南录自序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3闰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320328")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320328_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320328'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320328'>予自吴门，被命入卫，守独松关，乃王正二日，除浙西大制抚，领神皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320328_comment'></div>予辞尹，引<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1320328", 1320328, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>帐兵</span>二千人诣行在，日夕赞陈枢使宜中，谋迁三宫，分二王于闽、广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320328_comment'></div>元夕后，予所部兵皆聚于富阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320328_comment'></div>朝廷拟除予江东西、广东西制置大使，兼广东经略、知广州、湖南策应大使，未及出命，陈枢使已去国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320328_comment'></div>十九日，太皇除予右丞相兼枢密使、都督诸路军马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320328_comment'></div>时北兵驻高亭山，距脩门三十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320328_comment'></div>是日，虏帅即引董参政，以兵屯榷木教场，城中兵将官纷纷自往纳降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320328_comment'></div>予欲召富阳兵入城，已不及事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320328_comment'></div>三宫九庙，百万生灵，立有鱼肉之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320328_comment'></div>会使辙交驰，北约当国相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320328_comment'></div>诸执政、侍从聚于吴左丞相府，不知计所从出，交赞予一行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320328_comment'></div>国事至此，予不得爱身，且意北尚可以口舌动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320328_comment'></div>二十日，至高亭山，诘虏帅前后<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1320328", 1320328, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>失信</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320328_comment'></div>虏帅<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1320328", 1320328, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>辞屈</span>，且谓决不动三宫九庙，决不扰京城百姓，留予营中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320328_comment'></div>既而吕师孟来，予数骂其叔侄，愈不放还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320328_comment'></div>贾馀庆者，逢迎卖国，乘风旨使代予位，于是北兵入城，所以误吾国、陷吾民者，讲行无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320328_comment'></div>北知卖国非予所容也，相戒勿令文丞相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320328_comment'></div>未几，贾馀庆、吴坚、谢堂、家铉翁、刘岊，皆以府第为祈请使诣北方，盖空我朝廷，北将甘心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320328_comment'></div>二月八日，诸使登舟，忽北虏遣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1320328", 1320328, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>馆伴</span>逼予同往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320328_comment'></div>予被逼胁，欲即引决，又念未死以前，无非报国之日，姑隐忍就船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320328_comment'></div>方在京时，富阳兵已退趋婺、处等州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320328_comment'></div>予俟间还军，苦不自脱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320328_comment'></div>至是欲从道途谋遁，亦不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320328_comment'></div>至京口，留旬日，始得盐商小舟，于二月晦夜走真州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320328_comment'></div>朔日，守苗再成相见，论时事，慷慨流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320328_comment'></div>予致书两淮间，合兵兴复，苗赞之甚力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320328_comment'></div>初三日早，制司人来，乃出文书，谓丞相为赚城，欲不利于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320328_comment'></div>苗不以为然，送予出门，劝奔淮西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320328_comment'></div>予谓此北反间也，否则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1320328", 1320328, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>托辞</span>以逐客也，李公仁人，使见予必感动，遂之维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320328_comment'></div>苗遣五十兵四骑从行，夜抵西门，欲待旦求见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320328_comment'></div>呵卫严密，鼓角悲惨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320328_comment'></div>杜架阁谓李公必不可见，徒为矢石所陷，不如渡海归从王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320328_comment'></div>予然之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320328_comment'></div>自是日夜奔南，出入北冲，犯万万死，道途苦难，不可胜述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320328_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320328_comment'></div>予之得至淮也，使予与两淮合，北虏悬军深入，犯兵家大忌，可以计擒，江南一举而遂定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320328_comment'></div>天时不齐，人事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1320328", 1320328, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>好乖</span>，一夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1320328", 1320328, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>顿困</span>不足道，而国事不竞，哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320328_comment'></div>予至通，闻二王建元帅府于永嘉，陈枢使与张少保世杰方以李、郭之事为己任，狼狈憔悴之馀，喜不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1320328", 1320328, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>自制</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320328_comment'></div>跋涉鲸波，将蹑屩以从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320328_comment'></div>意者天之所以穷饿困乏而拂乱之者，其将有所俟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320328_comment'></div>德祐二年闰月日，庐陵文天祥自序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1320328_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3闰11日</a>　随行金应病卒。有诗吊唁。作品：《哭金路分应》<div id='poem_59181' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59181' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59181?labeling=true' target='_blank'>哭金路分应<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3闰11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59181")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59181_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59181'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59181'>我为吾君役，而从乃主行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59181'>险夷宁异趣，休戚与同情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59181'>遇贼能无死，寻医剧不生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59181'>通州一丘土，相望泪如倾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59181'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59181_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59180' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59180' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59180?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3闰11日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59180_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59180'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59180'>明朝吾渡海，汝魄在它乡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59180'>六七年华短，三千客路长。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59180'>招魂情黯黯，归骨事茫茫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59180'>有子应年长，平生不汝忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《指南录》卷三）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59180'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59180_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3闰</a>　本月葬金应于通州盐仓坝附近。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3闰</a>　闻说二王建帅府于温州，准备南归投奔。作品：《海船》<div id='poem_59522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海船</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3闰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59522")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_59522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_sentence_2_59522_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　本日开始发舟南下，沿海而行。一路有诗感怀记之。作品：《发通州》《石港》《卖鱼湾》《即事》（飘蓬一叶落天涯）《北海口》《出海》《渔舟》《扬子江》《使风》《苏洲洋》《过扬子江心》《入浙东》《夜潮》<div id='poem_58755' -----title
台州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='910fd35b66234007b61bac0c2184586c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("910fd35b66234007b61bac0c2184586c");'><span id='910fd35b66234007b61bac0c2184586c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>，41岁</div><div id='910fd35b66234007b61bac0c2184586c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>抵达台州城门镇，开始陆行步往温州。有诗记之。作品：《夜走》《绿绮堂》<div id='poem_59446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>夜走</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3闰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59446")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59446'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59446'>鲸波万里送归舟，倏忽惊心欲白头。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59446'>何处赭衣操剑戟，同时黄帽理兜鍪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59446'>人间风雨真成梦，夜半江山总是愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59446'>雁荡双峰片云隔，明朝蹑屩作清游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59446_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59446'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59446_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
黄岩（台州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='86f2907e20674c719876466a2b9fddbe_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("86f2907e20674c719876466a2b9fddbe");'><span id='86f2907e20674c719876466a2b9fddbe_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>，41岁</div><div id='86f2907e20674c719876466a2b9fddbe' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年3闰</a>　抵达台州城门镇，开始陆行步往温州。有诗记之。作品：《过黄岩》<div id='poem_58820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过黄岩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年3闰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_58820")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_58820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58820'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58820'>魏雎变张禄，越蠡改陶朱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58820'>谁料文山氏，姓刘名是洙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58820'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_58820_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a67e4fecf98f40d2a3c8f52cc47bfa3a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a67e4fecf98f40d2a3c8f52cc47bfa3a");'><span id='a67e4fecf98f40d2a3c8f52cc47bfa3a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>，41岁</div><div id='a67e4fecf98f40d2a3c8f52cc47bfa3a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年4月8日</a>　由城门镇步行约经过七八天时间，于本日抵达温州。作品：《至温州》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
福安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='55f982832a7247e5b51378a57d067ebc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("55f982832a7247e5b51378a57d067ebc");'><span id='55f982832a7247e5b51378a57d067ebc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>，41岁</div><div id='55f982832a7247e5b51378a57d067ebc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年5月26日</a>　在行都福安，除通议大夫、右丞相、枢密使，都督诸路军马，连上章拜辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　本年继续编写指南录，撰后序。作品：《指南录后序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作福州福安，据谭其骧地图改长溪。）</span><div id='poem_1320329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320329?labeling=true' target='_blank'>指南录后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320329")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320329'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320329'>德祐二年二月十九日，予除右丞相兼枢密使、都督诸路军马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320329_comment'></div>时北兵已迫脩门外，战、守、迁皆不及施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320329_comment'></div>缙绅大夫士萃于左丞相府，莫知计所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320329_comment'></div>会使辙交驰，北邀当国者相见，众谓予一行为可以纾祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320329_comment'></div>国事至此，予不得爱身，意北亦尚可以口舌动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320329_comment'></div>初，奉使往来，无留北者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320329_comment'></div>予更欲一觇北，归而求救国之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320329_comment'></div>于是辞相印不拜，翌日，以资政殿学士行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320329_comment'></div>初至北营，抗辞慷慨，上下颇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>惊动</span>，北亦未敢遽轻吾国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320329_comment'></div>不幸吕师孟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>构恶</span>于前，贾馀庆献谄于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320329_comment'></div>予羁縻不得还国，事遂不可收拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320329_comment'></div>予自度不得脱，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>直前</span>诟虏帅失信，数吕师孟叔侄为逆，但欲求死，不复顾利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320329_comment'></div>北虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>貌敬</span>，实则愤怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320329_comment'></div>二<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>贵酋</span>名曰馆伴，夜则以兵围所寓舍，而予不得归矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320329_comment'></div>未几，贾馀庆等以祈请使诣北，北驱予并往，而不在使者之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320329_comment'></div>予分当引决，然而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>隐忍</span>以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320329_comment'></div>昔人云：「将以有为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320329_comment'></div>至京口，得间奔真州，即具以北虚实告东西二阃，约以连兵大举，中兴机会，庶几在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320329_comment'></div>留二日，维扬帅下逐客之令，不得已，变姓名，诡踪迹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>草行露宿</span>，日与北骑相出没于长淮间，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>穷饿</span>无聊，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>追购</span>又急，天高地迥，号呼靡及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320329_comment'></div>已而得舟，避渚洲，出北海，然后渡扬子江，入苏州洋，展转四明、天台，以至于永嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320329_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320329_comment'></div>予之及于死者，不知其几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320329_comment'></div>诋大酋当死，骂逆贼当死，与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>贵酋</span>处二十日，争曲直，屡当死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320329_comment'></div>去京口，挟匕首以备不测，几自刭死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320329_comment'></div>经北舰十馀里，为巡船所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>物色</span>，几从鱼腹死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320329_comment'></div>真州逐之城门外，几徬徨死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320329_comment'></div>如扬州，过瓜洲扬子桥，竟使遇哨，无不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320329_comment'></div>扬州城下，进退不由，殆例送死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320329_comment'></div>坐桂公塘土围中，骑数千过其门，几落贼手死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320329_comment'></div>贾家庄几为巡徼所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>陵迫</span>死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320329_comment'></div>夜趋高邮，迷失道，几陷死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320329_comment'></div>质明，避哨竹林中，逻者数十骑，几无所逃死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320329_comment'></div>至高邮，制府檄下，几以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>捕系</span>死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320329_comment'></div>行城子河，出入乱尸中，舟与哨相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>后先</span>，几邂逅死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320329_comment'></div>至海陵，如高沙，常恐无辜死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320329_comment'></div>道海安、如皋，凡三百里，北与寇往来其间，无日而非可死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320329_comment'></div>至通州，几以不纳死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320329_comment'></div>以小舟涉鲸波，出无可奈何而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320329_comment'></div>固<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>付之度外</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320329_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320329_comment'></div>死生昼夜事也，死而死矣，而境界危恶，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>层见错出</span>，非人世所堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320329_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>痛定思痛</span>，痛何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320329_comment'></div>予在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>患难</span>中，间以诗记所遭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320329_comment'></div>今存其本不忍废，道中手自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/134/Comments/0")'>抄录</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1320329_comment'></div>使北营，留北关外，为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1320329_comment'></div>发北关外，历吴门、毗陵，渡瓜洲，复还京口，为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1320329_comment'></div>脱京口，趋真州、扬州、高邮、泰州、通州，为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1320329_comment'></div>自海道至永嘉，来三山，为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1320329_comment'></div>将藏之于家，使来者读之，悲予志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1320329_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1320329_comment'></div>予之生也幸，而幸生也何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1320329_comment'></div>所求乎为臣，主辱臣死有馀僇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1320329_comment'></div>所求乎为子，以父母之遗体行，殆而死，有馀责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1320329_comment'></div>将请罪于君，君不许；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1320329_comment'></div>请罪于母，母不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1320329_comment'></div>请罪于先人之墓，生无以救<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/166/Comments/0")'>国难</span>，死犹为厉鬼以击贼，义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1320329_comment'></div>赖天之灵，宗庙之福，脩我戈矛，从王于师，以为前驱，雪九庙之耻，复高祖之业，所谓誓不与贼俱生，所谓鞠躬尽力，死而后已，亦义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1320329_comment'></div>嗟夫，若予者，将无往而不得死所矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1320329_comment'></div>向也，使予委骨于草莽，予虽浩然无所愧怍，然微以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/186/Comments/0")'>自文</span>于君亲，君亲其谓予何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1320329_comment'></div>诚不自意返吾衣冠，重见日月，使旦夕得正丘首，复何憾哉，复何憾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1320329_comment'></div>是年夏五改元景炎，庐陵文天祥自序其诗，名曰《指南录》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1320329_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年7月4日</a>　从行都福安出发，准备再次聚兵抗元。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南平（南剑州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='49336aa284074eab9d94703d979d1908_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("49336aa284074eab9d94703d979d1908");'><span id='49336aa284074eab9d94703d979d1908_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>，41岁</div><div id='49336aa284074eab9d94703d979d1908' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年7月13日</a>　本日抵达，在南剑开府聚兵，再次抗元。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长汀
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e1cbeef57da14e09828543549bbd4f64_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e1cbeef57da14e09828543549bbd4f64");'><span id='e1cbeef57da14e09828543549bbd4f64_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>，41岁</div><div id='e1cbeef57da14e09828543549bbd4f64' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年11月</a>　率督府进入汀州长汀，继续调兵遣将，欲收复失地。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c875acb551e94f59a9e72a7307f74d96_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c875acb551e94f59a9e72a7307f74d96");'><span id='c875acb551e94f59a9e72a7307f74d96_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>，42岁</div><div id='c875acb551e94f59a9e72a7307f74d96' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年10月</a>　收拾散兵，并与母曾夫人、儿子道生等，再次辗转至汀州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a9cb361d56fd494d929c2e566f8c8a40_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a9cb361d56fd494d929c2e566f8c8a40");'><span id='a9cb361d56fd494d929c2e566f8c8a40_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>，41岁</div><div id='a9cb361d56fd494d929c2e566f8c8a40' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1276&endYear=1276')">1276年</a>　本年福州三山友人陈俞卒，为之痛哭。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
龙岩（漳州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='72e991b1f8de4eec91baa081d063eab4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("72e991b1f8de4eec91baa081d063eab4");'><span id='72e991b1f8de4eec91baa081d063eab4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>，42岁</div><div id='72e991b1f8de4eec91baa081d063eab4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年1月</a>　因前一年十一月后，觉汀州守黄去疾有异动，遂于本月移屯龙岩。拒绝李珏、王积翁报降书。作品：《正月书》<div id='poem_1320087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正月书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1277年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320087")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320087'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320087'>天祥皇恐，奉禀制使都承侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320087_comment'></div>天祥至汀后，即建、福以次沦失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320087_comment'></div>朝廷养士三百年，无死节者，如心先生差强人意，不知今果死否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320087_comment'></div>哀哉哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320087_comment'></div>坐孤城中，势力穷屈，泛观宇宙，无一可为，甚负吾平生之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320087_comment'></div>三年不见老母灯前，一夕，自汀移屯至龙岩，间道得与老母相见，即下从先帝游，复何云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320087_comment'></div>都相公去年馆伴，用情甚至，常念之不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320087_comment'></div>故回书，复遣罗辉来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320087_comment'></div>永诀永诀，伏乞台照。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1320087_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
梅州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='aa9795e0658b4e64a8c907a992c6983a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aa9795e0658b4e64a8c907a992c6983a");'><span id='aa9795e0658b4e64a8c907a992c6983a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>，42岁</div><div id='aa9795e0658b4e64a8c907a992c6983a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年3月</a>　移师梅洲，会见了母亲、妻子、儿女。授银青光禄大夫，职任依旧。肃立军政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年4月</a>　所部赵时赏、赵孟溁兵败退回闽西。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
会昌（赣州）

-----title
兴国
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7cda9e87ea9f48898e4a140c2188bdc6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7cda9e87ea9f48898e4a140c2188bdc6");'><span id='7cda9e87ea9f48898e4a140c2188bdc6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>，42岁</div><div id='7cda9e87ea9f48898e4a140c2188bdc6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年6月21日</a>　移师兴国，遣兵攻打赣州余地及吉州，斩杀伪天子黄从。此后附近州县响应，兴国军黄州新复，号令通于江淮。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永丰
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6828ba56abd54182be0b8e0de15da85a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6828ba56abd54182be0b8e0de15da85a");'><span id='6828ba56abd54182be0b8e0de15da85a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年</a>，42岁</div><div id='6828ba56abd54182be0b8e0de15da85a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1277&endYear=1277')">1277年8月17日</a>　六七月兵败后，移师永丰。本日于空坑遭元将李恒部袭击围困，夫人、一子、二女不知所踪。部将多有折损。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
龙川（循州）

-----end



-----title
海丰
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1952411fe44e4c8f83a8a4223198b898_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1952411fe44e4c8f83a8a4223198b898");'><span id='1952411fe44e4c8f83a8a4223198b898_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年</a>，43岁</div><div id='1952411fe44e4c8f83a8a4223198b898' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年2月</a>　进兵惠州，驻兵海丰县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年3月</a>　仍驻兵海丰，屯兵丽江浦，命弟文璧攻打惠州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年5月</a>　本月始闻端宗驾崩凶问以及祥兴帝登极讯。奉表有贺并自劾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年5月25日</a>　文璧弟以秘阁修撰、枢密副使都承制、江西转运副使、兼参谋权户部尚书，总领广东赋富，兼知惠州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年6月</a>　督府随行朝至厓山也转移至广州，进驻船澳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年8月</a>　授少保、信国公，职任依旧，母曾氏进封齐魏国夫人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年9月7日</a>　本日寅时，母齐魏国夫人薨于船澳行督府。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a720c3b32f474658a4d43a90b328a7fc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a720c3b32f474658a4d43a90b328a7fc");'><span id='a720c3b32f474658a4d43a90b328a7fc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年</a>，43岁</div><div id='a720c3b32f474658a4d43a90b328a7fc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年12月15日</a>　再次移师趋向海丰，入南岭，谋据险自固。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年12月20日</a>　于海丰县境内五坡岭遭敌将张弘范部袭击，被俘。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
潮阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d7b7b5d925e74906a287cd437a2536da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d7b7b5d925e74906a287cd437a2536da");'><span id='d7b7b5d925e74906a287cd437a2536da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年</a>，43岁</div><div id='d7b7b5d925e74906a287cd437a2536da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年10月</a>　举兵讨陈懿，攻刘兴，率部进驻潮阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年11月7日</a>　长子道生病卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年11月</a>　以两子皆殁，书弟文璧立其次子文升为继子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年12月</a>　调遣江西入广的邹氵凤、刘子俊征讨陈懿党。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='23eccacfc09349dd86fdb0db26396f2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("23eccacfc09349dd86fdb0db26396f2b");'><span id='23eccacfc09349dd86fdb0db26396f2b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1279')">1278-1279年</a>，43-44岁</div><div id='23eccacfc09349dd86fdb0db26396f2b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1278&endYear=1278')">1278年12月27日</a>　被俘至潮阳见张弘范，抗节不屈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年1月2日</a>　元将张弘范胁迫下海于舟中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年1月6日</a>　本日从潮阳出发，趋向厓山。<br /></div>
-----end

id='poem_59289' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59289' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59289?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二月六日海上大战国事不济孤臣天祥坐北舟中向南恸哭为之诗曰</a><span id='poem_sentence_6_59289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59289'>间关归国洗日光，白麻重宣不敢当。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59289_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
广州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c08de282144340f49b59fb2bb1a85ca4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c08de282144340f49b59fb2bb1a85ca4");'><span id='c08de282144340f49b59fb2bb1a85ca4_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年3月13日</a>　本日坐元舟抵达广州城。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年3月14日</a>　元将张弘范设宴劝降，拒绝之。作品：《张元帅谓予国已亡矣杀身以忠谁复书之予谓商非不亡夷齐自不食周粟人臣自尽其心岂论书与不书张为改容因成一诗》<div id='poem_59112' class='_poem'><div
