class='authorDate'>（1279年3月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59112")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59112_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59112'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59112'>高人名若浼，烈士死如归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59112'>智灭犹吞炭，商亡正采薇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59112'>岂因徼后福，其肯蹈危机。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59112'>万古春秋义，悠悠双泪挥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59112'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59112_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年4月16日</a>　撰写《指南后录·序》作品：《指南录后序》<div id='poem_1320329' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320329' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320329?labeling=true' target='_blank'>指南录后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1276年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320329")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320329_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320329'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320329'>德祐二年二月十九日，予除右丞相兼枢密使、都督诸路军马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320329_comment'></div>时北兵已迫脩门外，战、守、迁皆不及施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320329_comment'></div>缙绅大夫士萃于左丞相府，莫知计所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320329_comment'></div>会使辙交驰，北邀当国者相见，众谓予一行为可以纾祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320329_comment'></div>国事至此，予不得爱身，意北亦尚可以口舌动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320329_comment'></div>初，奉使往来，无留北者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320329_comment'></div>予更欲一觇北，归而求救国之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320329_comment'></div>于是辞相印不拜，翌日，以资政殿学士行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320329_comment'></div>初至北营，抗辞慷慨，上下颇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>惊动</span>，北亦未敢遽轻吾国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320329_comment'></div>不幸吕师孟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>构恶</span>于前，贾馀庆献谄于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320329_comment'></div>予羁縻不得还国，事遂不可收拾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320329_comment'></div>予自度不得脱，则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>直前</span>诟虏帅失信，数吕师孟叔侄为逆，但欲求死，不复顾利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320329_comment'></div>北虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>貌敬</span>，实则愤怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320329_comment'></div>二<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>贵酋</span>名曰馆伴，夜则以兵围所寓舍，而予不得归矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320329_comment'></div>未几，贾馀庆等以祈请使诣北，北驱予并往，而不在使者之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320329_comment'></div>予分当引决，然而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>隐忍</span>以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320329_comment'></div>昔人云：「将以有为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320329_comment'></div>至京口，得间奔真州，即具以北虚实告东西二阃，约以连兵大举，中兴机会，庶几在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1320329_comment'></div>留二日，维扬帅下逐客之令，不得已，变姓名，诡踪迹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>草行露宿</span>，日与北骑相出没于长淮间，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>穷饿</span>无聊，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>追购</span>又急，天高地迥，号呼靡及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1320329_comment'></div>已而得舟，避渚洲，出北海，然后渡扬子江，入苏州洋，展转四明、天台，以至于永嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1320329_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1320329_comment'></div>予之及于死者，不知其几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1320329_comment'></div>诋大酋当死，骂逆贼当死，与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>贵酋</span>处二十日，争曲直，屡当死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1320329_comment'></div>去京口，挟匕首以备不测，几自刭死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1320329_comment'></div>经北舰十馀里，为巡船所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>物色</span>，几从鱼腹死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1320329_comment'></div>真州逐之城门外，几徬徨死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1320329_comment'></div>如扬州，过瓜洲扬子桥，竟使遇哨，无不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1320329_comment'></div>扬州城下，进退不由，殆例送死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1320329_comment'></div>坐桂公塘土围中，骑数千过其门，几落贼手死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1320329_comment'></div>贾家庄几为巡徼所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>陵迫</span>死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1320329_comment'></div>夜趋高邮，迷失道，几陷死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1320329_comment'></div>质明，避哨竹林中，逻者数十骑，几无所逃死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1320329_comment'></div>至高邮，制府檄下，几以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/106/Comments/0")'>捕系</span>死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1320329_comment'></div>行城子河，出入乱尸中，舟与哨相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>后先</span>，几邂逅死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1320329_comment'></div>至海陵，如高沙，常恐无辜死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1320329_comment'></div>道海安、如皋，凡三百里，北与寇往来其间，无日而非可死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1320329_comment'></div>至通州，几以不纳死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1320329_comment'></div>以小舟涉鲸波，出无可奈何而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1320329_comment'></div>固<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/122/Comments/0")'>付之度外</span>矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1320329_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1320329_comment'></div>死生昼夜事也，死而死矣，而境界危恶，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>层见错出</span>，非人世所堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1320329_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/129/Comments/0")'>痛定思痛</span>，痛何如哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1320329_comment'></div>予在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/131/Comments/0")'>患难</span>中，间以诗记所遭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1320329_comment'></div>今存其本不忍废，道中手自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/134/Comments/0")'>抄录</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1320329_comment'></div>使北营，留北关外，为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1320329_comment'></div>发北关外，历吴门、毗陵，渡瓜洲，复还京口，为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1320329_comment'></div>脱京口，趋真州、扬州、高邮、泰州、通州，为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1320329_comment'></div>自海道至永嘉，来三山，为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1320329_comment'></div>将藏之于家，使来者读之，悲予志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1320329_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1320329_comment'></div>予之生也幸，而幸生也何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1320329_comment'></div>所求乎为臣，主辱臣死有馀僇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1320329_comment'></div>所求乎为子，以父母之遗体行，殆而死，有馀责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1320329_comment'></div>将请罪于君，君不许；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1320329_comment'></div>请罪于母，母不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1320329_comment'></div>请罪于先人之墓，生无以救<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/166/Comments/0")'>国难</span>，死犹为厉鬼以击贼，义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1320329_comment'></div>赖天之灵，宗庙之福，脩我戈矛，从王于师，以为前驱，雪九庙之耻，复高祖之业，所谓誓不与贼俱生，所谓鞠躬尽力，死而后已，亦义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1320329_comment'></div>嗟夫，若予者，将无往而不得死所矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1320329_comment'></div>向也，使予委骨于草莽，予虽浩然无所愧怍，然微以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1320329", 1320329, "Clauses/186/Comments/0")'>自文</span>于君亲，君亲其谓予何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1320329_comment'></div>诚不自意返吾衣冠，重见日月，使旦夕得正丘首，复何憾哉，复何憾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1320329_comment'></div>是年夏五改元景炎，庐陵文天祥自序其诗，名曰《指南录》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1320329_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年4月22日</a>　本日乘船离开广州北上。有诗感之。作品：《出广州第一宿》<div id='poem_59326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>出广州第一宿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年4月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59326")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59326'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59326'>越王台下路，搔首叹萍踪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59326'>城古都招水，山高易得风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59326'>鼓声残雨后，塔影暮林中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59326'>一样连营火，山同河不同。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59326_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59326'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59326_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

英德

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年4月</a>　进入英德府县境内，有诗记之。作品：《英德道中》《晚渡》《珊瑚吟》<div id='poem_59156' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59156' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_1_59156'>乾坤正风雨，轩冕总泥途。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59156'>自叹鸢肩薄，谁怜鹤影孤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59156'>少年狂不醒，夜夜梦伊吾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59156'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59156_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59231?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚渡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_59231'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59231'>青山围万叠，流落此何邦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59231'>云静龙归海，风清马渡江。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59231'>汲滩供茗碗，编竹当蓬窗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59231'>一井沙头月，羁鸿共影双。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59231'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59231_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59476' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59476' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59476?labeling=true' target='_blank'>珊瑚吟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_59476'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59476'>南方有珍禽，鸣声天下奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59476'>毛羽黑如漆，两脸<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作眼）</span>凝璚脂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59476'>燕赵佳公子，笼槛以自随。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59476'>童子重丁宁，饮食必以时。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59476'>将献上林苑，来巢万年枝。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59476'>待之岂少恩，不免加絷维。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59476'>珊瑚真珊瑚，碎琢良自悲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59476'>中原寒气深，风土非所宜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59476_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59476'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_59476_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年5月</a>　端午前后，与邓光荐有唱和。作品：《和中甫端午韵不依次》《又呈中斋》<div id='poem_59125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和中甫端午韵不依次</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59125")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59125'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59125'>黄茅古道外，羸马发南州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59125'>有客嗤齐鲁<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作虏）</span>，何人念楚囚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59125'>岁年付流水，风雨满沧洲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59125'>手把菖蒲看，黑头非所求。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58972' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/58972?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又呈中斋<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_58972")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_58972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58972'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58972'>风雨羊肠道，飘零万死身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58972'>牛儿朝共载，木客夜为邻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_58972'>庾子江南梦<span class='inlineComment2'>（韩本作客）</span>，苏郎海上贫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_58972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_58972'>悠悠看晚渡，谁是济川人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_58972_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_58972'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_58972_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_58973' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_58973' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_58973_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_58973'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_58973'>万里论心晚，相看慰乱离。<div id='poem_sentence_0_58973_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_58973'>丹成俄已化，璧碎尚无缁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_58973_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年5月18日</a>　过宿韶州南华寺，慨叹六祖真身遭乱兵窃胸探心之祸。作品：《南华山》<div id='poem_59467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59467' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59467")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59467'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59467'>北行近千里，迷复忘西东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59467'>行行至南华，忽忽如梦中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59467'>佛化知几尘，患乃与我同。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59467'>有形终归灭，不灭惟真空。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_59467'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_59467_0'>⑴ 自注：六祖禅师真身，盖数百年矣，为乱兵刲其心肝。乃知有患难，佛不免，况人乎。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_59467_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

芜湖

马鞍山（太平州）

南京

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年6月13日</a>　一同抵达建康的邓光荐因病寓留天庆观，不行。作品：《怀中甫 时中甫以病寓留天庆观》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年7月27日</a>　七月壬申，为难友邓光荐集题名《东海集》并作序。作品：《东海集序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（具体日期由录者推定。）</span><div id='poem_1320333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东海集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年7月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320333")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320333'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320333'>《东海集》者，友人客海南以来诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320333_comment'></div>海南诗而曰《东海集》者何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320333_comment'></div>鲁仲连天下士，友人之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320333_comment'></div>友人自为举子时，已大肆力于诗，于诸大家皆尝登其门而涉其流，其本赡，其养锐，故所诣特深到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320333_comment'></div>余尝评其诗，浑涵有英气，鍜鍊如自然，美则美矣，犹未免有意于为诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320333_comment'></div>自丧乱后，友人挈其家，避地游官岭海，而全家毁于盗，孤穷流落，困顿万状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320333_comment'></div>然后崖山除礼部侍郎，中且权直学士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320333_comment'></div>会南风不竞，御舟漂散，友人仓卒蹈海者，再为北军所钩致，遂不获死，以至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320333_comment'></div>凡十数年间，可惊可愕，可悲可愤，可痛可闷之事，友人备尝，无所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320333_comment'></div>其惨戚感慨之气，结而不信，皆于诗乎发之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320333_comment'></div>盖至是动乎情性，自不能不诗，杜子美夔州、柳子厚柳州以后文字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320333_comment'></div>余与友人年相若，又同里闬，以斯文相好，然平生落落不相及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320333_comment'></div>及居楚囚中，而友人在行，同患难者数月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320333_comment'></div>其自五羊至金陵所赋，皆予目击，或相唱和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320333_comment'></div>时余坐金陵驿，无所作为，乃取友人诸诗，笔之于书，与相关者并附焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320333_comment'></div>后之览者因诗以见吾二人之志，其必有感慨于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320333_comment'></div>己卯七月壬申，文天祥叙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1320333_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年7月</a>　于金陵驿馆壁见王清惠《满江红》词有感，有词记之。（燕子楼中）<span id='poem_sentence_1_59038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59038'>江山如梦耳，天地柰愁何。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年8月25日</a>　舟行途中，有感，以诗记之。作品：《江行有感》<div id='poem_59078' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59078' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59078?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江行有感<span class='inlineComment2'>（二十五日）</span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_59078'>蒲萄肥汗马，荆棘冷铜驼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59078_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59078'>巫峡朝云湿，洞庭秋水波。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59078'>莫恨吾生误，江东<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_59078", 59078, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>才俊</span>多。<div -----title
宝应
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d13ea7668d1d4402ad590e5ce9c8deef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d13ea7668d1d4402ad590e5ce9c8deef");'><span id='d13ea7668d1d4402ad590e5ce9c8deef_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>本日从高邮出发，继续北上，经过宝应，有诗记之。作品：《发高邮》《宝应道中》<div id='poem_59343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_59343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59343'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59343'>初出高沙门，轻舫绕城楼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59343'>一水何曲折，百年此绸缪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59343'>北望渺无际，飞鸟翔平畴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59343'>寒芜入荒落，日薄行人愁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59343'>行行行湖曲，万顷涵清秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59343'>大风吹樯倒，如荡彭蠡舟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59343'>欲寄故乡泪，使入长江流。<div "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>篙人</span>为我言，此水通淮头。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59343'>前与黄河合，同作沧海沤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59343'>踟蹰忽失意，拭泪泪不收。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59343'>吴会日已远，回首重悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59343'>驰驱梁赵郊，壮士何离忧。<div id='poem_sentence_11_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_59343'>吾道久矣<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>东，陆沈古神州。<div id='poem_sentence_12_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_59343'>我今戴南冠，何异有北投。<div id='poem_sentence_13_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_59343'>不能裂肝脑，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_59343", 59343, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>直气</span>摩斗牛。<div id='poem_sentence_14_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_59343'>但愿光岳合，休明复商周。<div id='poem_sentence_15_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_59343'>不使殊方魄，终为异物羞。<div id='poem_sentence_16_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_59343'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_59343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_59343'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_59343_0'>⑴ 韩本、四库本作已</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_59343_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_59145' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59145' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59145?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宝应道中</a><span id='poem_sentence_0_59145'>天阔抟南雁，淮途长北驱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59145'>甘棠成传舍，细柳作康衢。<div -----title
淮安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a2269db9772245ada2bed780feb4c7c1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a2269db9772245ada2bed780feb4c7c1");'><span id='a2269db9772245ada2bed780feb4c7c1_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年9月1日</a>　本日抵达淮安军，夜宿阚石，有诗记之。作品：《淮安军》<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作淮安军，据谭其骧地图改楚州。）</span>《过淮河宿阚石有感》<div id='poem_59542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59542?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮安军<span class='inlineComment2'>（九月一日）</span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_59542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59542'>岂无匹妇冤，定无万夫雄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59542'>中原在其北，登城望何穷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59542'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59542_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59402?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_59402'>北征垂半年，依依只南土。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59402'>今晨渡淮河，始觉非故宇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59402'>江乡已无家，三年一羁旅。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59402'>龙翔在何方，乃我妻子所。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59402'>昔也无柰何，忽已置念虑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59402'>今行日已近，使我泪如雨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59402'>我为纲常谋，有身不得顾。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59402'>妻兮莫望夫，子兮莫望父。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59402'>天长与地久，此恨极千古。<div id='poem_sentence_8_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59402'>来生业缘在，骨肉当如故。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59402_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59402'></div><div id='poem_59345' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59345' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59345?labeling=true' target='_blank'>发淮安<span class='inlineComment2'>（九月二日）</span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_59345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59345'>烟火无一家，荒草青漫漫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59345'>恍如泛沧海，身坐玻瓈盘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59345'>时时逢北人，什伍扶征鞍。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59345'>云我戍江南，当军身属官。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59345'>北人适吴楚，所忧地少寒。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59345'>江南有游子，风雪上燕山。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59345'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_59345_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

宿迁

邳州

韩本、四库本作向来</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_59516_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

沛县（滕州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4ff044c2d98d483088f388b08567c74a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4ff044c2d98d483088f388b08567c74a");'><span id='4ff044c2d98d483088f388b08567c74a_link' id='poem_sentence_0_59420_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59420'>王侯与将相，不出徐济间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59420_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_59603'>永言三侯章，隐隐闻儿童。<div id='poem_sentence_12_59603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_59603'>叶落皆归根，飘零独秋蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_13_59603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_59603'>登台共悽恻，目送<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>南飞鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_14_59603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_59603'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_59603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_59603'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_59603_0'>⑴ 原作之，据韩本、四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_59603_comment'></div></div><br /></div>

东阿

id='poem_sentence_11_59339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_59339'>太阳经天行，大化不暂留。<div id='poem_sentence_12_59339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59352'>一朝渔阳动鼙鼓，大河<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>以北无<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_2_59352'>公家兄弟奋戈起，一十七郡连<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_59352", 59352, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>夏盟</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59352'>贼闻失色<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_59352", 59352, id='poem_sentence_3_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59352'>明皇父子将西狩，由是灵武起义兵。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59352'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_59352", 59352, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>唐家</span>再造<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_59352", 59352, "Clauses/10/Comments/1")'>李郭</span>力，若论牵制公威灵。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59352'>哀哉常山惨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_59352", 59352, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>钩舌</span>，心归朝廷气不慑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59352'>崎岖坎坷不得志，出入四朝老<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_59352", 59352, id='poem_sentence_8_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59352'>希烈安能遽杀公，宰相卢杞欺日月。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59352_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59352'>公死于今六百年，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_59352", 59352, -----title
德州（景州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3165d6d8f05f4b9e9be08a848f7eed13_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3165d6d8f05f4b9e9be08a848f7eed13");'><span id='3165d6d8f05f4b9e9be08a848f7eed13_link' id='poem_title_59599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59599'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59599'>三年戎服行，五岭文玉会。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59599'>跻攀上崖磴，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_59599", 59599, id='poem_sentence_9_59599'>兹游冠平生，天宇更宏大。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59599'>心与太虚际，目空九围内。<div id='poem_sentence_10_59599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59599'>男儿不出居，妇人坐帷盖。<div id='poem_sentence_11_59599_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 清苑（保州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='970e0373606b4f119b0c1e05c297c338_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("970e0373606b4f119b0c1e05c297c338");'><span id='970e0373606b4f119b0c1e05c297c338_link' id='poem_sentence_0_59463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59463'>白云何渺渺，天地何茫茫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59463'>山川一今古，人物几兴亡。<div id='poem_sentence_11_59463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_59463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_59463'>天地行日月，万代乘景光。<div id='poem_sentence_17_59463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_59463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_59463'>来者不可见，远游赋彷徨。<div id='poem_sentence_20_59463_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
徐水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bfff036f9b9b4dc98f698b8b8aae5539_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bfff036f9b9b4dc98f698b8b8aae5539");'><span id='bfff036f9b9b4dc98f698b8b8aae5539_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年</a>，44岁</div><div id='bfff036f9b9b4dc98f698b8b8aae5539' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>本日从保州出发，过安肃州梁门（徐水）。有诗记之。作品：《保涿州三诗·赵太祖墓》《过梁门》<div id='poem_59464' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59464' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59464?labeling=true' target='_blank'>保涿州三诗<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>赵太祖墓<span class='inlineComment2'>（在保州，二十九日起三十日到）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年9月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59464")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59464_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59464'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59464'>我行保州塞，御河直其东。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59464'>山川犹有灵，佳气何郁葱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59464'>顾我巾车囚<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作因，据韩本、四库本改）</span>，厉气转秋蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59464'>瓣香欲往拜，惆怅临长空。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59464_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59464'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59464_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_59097' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59097' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59097?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过梁门</a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年9月29日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59097")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59097_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59097'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59097'>一一金瓯在，双双镇璧全。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59097_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59097'>土花开旧国，风絮渡江船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59097_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59097'>南北分新统，江淮号极边。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59097_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59097'>更和天堑失，回首惨啼鹃。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59097_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59097'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59097_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
涿州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9c12577a8a464db48a71d7282e5e1837_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9c12577a8a464db48a71d7282e5e1837");'><span id='9c12577a8a464db48a71d7282e5e1837_link' -----title
北京
-----detail

id='poem_sentence_1_59404'>游子衣裳如<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>铁冷，残星荒店野鸡啼<span class='inlineComment2'>（原校：一作乱鸣鸡）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59404_comment'></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年10月5日</a>　昔日同僚部下前来拜访或劝降，皆无功而返。本日午后移至兵马司土牢。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_59004'>朝餐淡薄神还爽，夜睡崎岖梦自安。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59004_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59004'>亡国大夫谁为传，祇饶野史与人看。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1279&endYear=1279')">1279年11月10日</a>　冬至日后，自以为见杀，但久无消息，不闻元人意向。<br /><a href="javascript: href='/Writing/1320090?labeling=true' target='_blank'>狱中与弟书<span class='inlineComment2'>（祥兴二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1279年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_1320090_comment'></div>及出南安，系吾颈，絷吾足，于是不食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320090_comment'></div>将谓及吉州则死，首丘之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320090_comment'></div>乃五日过吉，又三日过丰城，无饭八日，不知饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320090_comment'></div>既过吉，思之无义，且尚在江南，或尚有生意，遂入建康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320090_comment'></div>居七十馀日，果有忠义人约夺我于江上，盖真州境也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320090_comment'></div>及期失约，惘然北行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320090_comment'></div>道中求死，无其间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320090_comment'></div>入幽州，下之狴犴，枷颈锁手，节其饮食，今已二十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320090_comment'></div>吾舍生取义，无可言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320090_comment'></div>今千万寄此及诗达吾弟，盖绝笔也。</div><div href='/Writing/1320330?labeling=true' target='_blank'>指南后录卷一下跋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1280年1月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320330")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320330_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320330'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320330'>此册为《指南后录》第一卷下，第二卷起八月二十四日《发建康》，终《岁除有感》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320330_comment'></div>尚有《零丁洋》诸诗及《后录》本在惠州，合隶为一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320330_comment'></div>而所恨者，《指南前录》叙号存，而诗已不完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320330_comment'></div>侍郎弟姑据所存本，使不泯于世，一联半句，使天下见之，识其为人，即吾死无憾矣，况篇帙之多乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320330_comment'></div>岁在庚辰正月二十日，文山履善甫书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1320330_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1280&endYear=1280')">1280年</a>　初春，北京土牢中获女儿柳娘书，始得儿女消息，赋诗回函言衷肠。作品：《指南后录·得儿女消息》<br class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59335'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59335'>君不见常山太守骂羯奴，天津桥上舌尽刳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59335'>又不见睢阳将军怒切齿，三十六人同日死。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59335'>去冬长至前一日，朔庭呼我弗为屈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59335'>丈夫开口即见胆，意谓生死在顷刻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59335'>赭衣冉冉生苍苔，书云时节忽复来。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59335'>鬼影青灯照孤坐，梦啼死血丹心破。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59335'>只今便作渭水囚，食粟已是西山羞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59335'>悔不当年跳东海，空有鲁连心独在。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59335'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_59335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_content_1320091'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320091'>潭卢之西坑有一地，已印元渭阳所献月形下角穴，第浅露非其正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320091_comment'></div>其右山上有穴，可买以藏我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320091_comment'></div>如骨不可归，招魂以封之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320091_comment'></div>升子嗣续，吾死奚憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320091_comment'></div>女弟一家流落在此，可为悲痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320091_comment'></div>吾弟同气取之，名正言顺，宜极力出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320091_comment'></div>自广达建康，日与中甫邓先生居，具知吾心事，吾铭当以属之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320091_comment'></div>若时未可出，则姑藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320091_comment'></div>将来文山宜作一寺，我庙于其中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1320091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1320091'><span id='poem_sentence_1_59317'>今年后三夕，大雨复没床。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59317'>我辞江海来，中原路茫茫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59317'>舟楫不复见，车马驰康庄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59317'>矧居<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_59317", 59317, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>圜土</span>中，得水<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>犹得浆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59317'>忽如巨石<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>浸，仓卒殊徬徨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59317'>明星尚未启，大风方发狂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59317'>叫呼人不应，宛转水中央。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59317'>壁下有水穴，群鼠走踉蹡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59317'>或如鱼泼剌，垫溺无所藏。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59317'>周身莫如物，患至不得防。<div id='poem_sentence_10_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59317'>业为世间人，何处逃祸殃。<div id='poem_sentence_11_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_59317'>朝来辟<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作开）</span>沟道，宛如决陂塘。<div id='poem_sentence_17_59317'>羁栖无复望<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上五字原缺，据四库本补）</span>，坐待仆且僵。<div id='poem_sentence_17_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_59317'>乾坤莽空阔，何为此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_59317", 59317, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>凉凉</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_18_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_59317'>达人识义命，此事关纲常。<div id='poem_sentence_19_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_59317'>万物方焦枯，皇皇祷穹苍。<div id='poem_sentence_20_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_59317'>上帝实好生，夜半下龙章。<div id='poem_sentence_21_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_59317'>但愿天下人，家家足稻粱。<div id='poem_sentence_22_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_59317'>我命浑小事，我死庸何伤。<div id='poem_sentence_23_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_59317'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_59317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_59317'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_59317_0'>⑴ 原作冰，据韩本、四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_59317_0'>⑵ 韩本、四库本作避巨</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_59317_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_59593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>筑房子歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59593")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59593'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59593'>自予居狴犴，一室以自治。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59593'>二年二大雨，地污实成池。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59593'>圄人为我恻，畚土以筑之。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59593'>筑之可二尺，宛然水中坻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59593'>初运朽壤来，臭秽恨莫追。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59593'>掩鼻不可近，牛皂鸡于埘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59593'>须臾传黑坟，千杵鸣参差。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59593'>但见如坻平，粪土不复疑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59593'>乃知天下事，不在论镃基。<div id='poem_sentence_8_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59593'>苟可掩耳目，臭腐誇神奇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59593'>世人所不辨，羊质而虎皮。<div id='poem_sentence_10_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59593'>大者莫不然，小者又何知。<div id='poem_sentence_11_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_59593'>深居守我玄，默观道推移。<div id='poem_sentence_12_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_59593'>何时蝉蜕去，忽与浊世违。<div id='poem_sentence_13_59593_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_59593'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_59593_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年5月</a>　书函与舅家，嘱咐后事。作品：《燕山与外氏书》<div id='poem_1320085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>燕山与外氏书</a><span class='authorDate'>（至元十八年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320085")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320085_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320085'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320085'>甥天祥百拜，覆梅溪尊舅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320085_comment'></div>天祥为子不孝，老母已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320085_comment'></div>诵「如母存焉」之诗，今惟此一舅，间阔以来，思慕所及，每一南望，盖未尝不为之潸然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320085_comment'></div>天祥自国难以来，以为为臣死忠，古今通义，故间关兵革，鞠躬尽力，百折而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320085_comment'></div>天命不时，卒以丧败，家国俱弊，谓之何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320085_comment'></div>当仓皇时，仰药不剂，身落人手，死生竟不自由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320085_comment'></div>及至朔廷，抗辞决命，乃留连幽囚，旷阅年岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320085_comment'></div>孟子曰：「夭寿不贰，修身以俟之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320085_comment'></div>如此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320085_comment'></div>老母年方望七，客殡馀憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320085_comment'></div>然生荣死哀，粗慰人子之志，以此虽刀锯在前，故应含笑入地耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320085_comment'></div>母丧归葬，已戒仲氏，不肖孤不能躬毕大事，负此悲痛，天地鬼神谅昭鉴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320085_comment'></div>八哥来，伏谂尊候万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320085_comment'></div>然终年不得与八哥一相见，今且告归，仰惟德人动履，神物护持，优游馀年，万万珍重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320085_comment'></div>儿子道生不幸夭折，今立升侄为子，凡百惟舅翁教之诲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1320085_comment'></div>区区朽骨，已恨沟壑，当具衣冠，藏于文山之北，畴昔舅所指处也，并哀而窆之是望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1320085_comment'></div>谨奉书永诀，万古万古，不备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1320085_comment'></div>辛巳夏五，甥天祥百拜覆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1320085_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1320085'><span class='label'>按：</span>元刘将孙《养吾斋集》卷二六，影印文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1320085_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年6月</a>　本时期，作正气歌以明志。作品：《正气歌》<div id='poem_59353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59353' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59353?labeling=true' target='_blank'>正气歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59353")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59353_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_59353'>予囚北庭，坐一土室，室广八尺，深可四寻，单扉低小，白间短窄，污下而幽暗。当此夏日，诸气萃然：雨潦四集，浮动床几，时则为水气；涂泥半朝，蒸沤历澜，时则为土气；乍晴暴热，风道四塞，时则为日气；檐阴薪爨，助长炎虐，时则为火气；仓腐寄顿，陈陈逼人，时则为米气；骈肩杂遝，腥臊污垢，时则为人气；或圊溷，或毁尸，或腐鼠，恶气杂出，时则为秽气。叠是数气，当侵沴鲜不为厉。而予以孱弱，俯仰其间，于兹二年矣，无恙。是殆有养致然尔。然尔亦安知所养何哉。孟子曰：「吾善养吾浩然之气。」彼气有七，吾气有一，以一敌七，吾何患焉。况浩然者，乃天地之正气也。作《正气歌》一首。</div><div id='poem_preface_59353_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59353'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59353'>天地有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_59353", 59353, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>正气</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_59353", 59353, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>杂然</span>赋<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_59353", 59353, "Clauses/1/Comments/1")'>流形</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59353'>下则为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_59353", 59353, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>河岳</span>，上则为日星。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59353'>于人曰浩然，沛乎塞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_59353", 59353, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>苍冥</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59353'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_59353", 59353, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>皇路</span>当清夷，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_59353", 59353, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>含和</span>吐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_59353", 59353, onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_59353", 59353, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>董狐笔</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_59353", 59353, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>清操</span>厉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_59353", 59353, id='poem_note_59353_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年</a>　本年夏，文璧与文懿孙来探访，与之诀别，并嘱咐后事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年7月2日</a>　本日燕京大雨，有诗记之。作品：《七月二日大雨歌》<div id='poem_59286' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59286' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59286?labeling=true' target='_blank'>七月二日大雨歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年7月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59286")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_59286_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59286'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59286'>燕山五六月，气候苦不常。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59286'>积阴绵五旬，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_59286", 59286, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>畏景</span>淡无光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59286'>天漏比西极，地湿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>等南方。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59286'>今何苦常雨，昔何苦常旸。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59286'>七月二日夜，天工为谁忙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59286'>浮云黑如墨，飘风怒如狂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59286'>滂沱至夜半，天地为低昂。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_59286'>势如蛟龙出，平陆俄怀襄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59286'>初疑倒巫峡，又似翻潇湘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59286'>千门各已闭，仰视天茫茫。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59286'>但闻屋侧声，人力无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_59286", 59286, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>支当</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59286'>嗟哉此圜土，占胜非高冈。<div id='poem_sentence_11_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_59286'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_59286", 59286, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>赭衣</span>无容足，南房并北房。<div id='poem_sentence_12_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_59286'>北房水二尺，聚立唯东箱<span class='inlineComment2'>（韩本、四库本作厢）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_59286'>桎梏犹自可，凛然覆穹墙。<div id='poem_sentence_14_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_59286'>南冠者为谁，独居沮洳场。<div id='poem_sentence_17_59286_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年7月</a>　京师大雨，所处兵马司墙坏脱落，转移至司宫籍监，条件有所改善。有诗多篇。作品：《咏怀》《偶成》《移司即事》《不睡》《宫籍监》<div id='poem_59443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59443' "Clauses/0/Comments/1")'>烹然</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（韩本、四库本作煎）</span>，天地一釜鬵<span class='inlineComment2'>（原误作灊）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59443_comment'></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年7月11日</a>　本日又回到旧兵马司，改换移至另一室，地势较高，干燥空凉。作品：《还司即事》<div id='poem_59428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59428' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年8月7日</a>　本日又回到故处土牢，依然臭秽蒸湿，条件恶劣。作品：《还狱》<div id='poem_59429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_59429'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59429'>人情感故物，百年多离忧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59429'>桑下住三宿，应者犹迟留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59429'>矧兹方丈室，屏居二春秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59429'>夜眠与昼坐，隤乎安楚囚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59429'>自罹大雨水，圜土俱荡舟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_59429'>此身委传舍，迁徙无定谋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_59429'>去之已旬月，宫室重绸缪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_59429'>故家不可复，故国已成丘。<div id='poem_sentence_9_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_59429'>对此重回首，汪然涕泗流。<div id='poem_sentence_10_59429_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_59429'>人生如空花，随风任飘浮。<div id='poem_title_59159' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/59159?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雨雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1281年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_59159")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59159_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59159'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59159'>秋色金台路，殷殷半马蹄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59159'>因风随作雪，有雨便成泥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59159'>过眼惊新梦，伤心忆旧题。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59159'>江云愁万叠，遗恨鹧鸪啼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59159'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59159_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1281&endYear=1281')">1281年12月30日</a>　本日除夕，有诗感怀。作品：《除夜》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年1月1日</a>　撰写《集杜诗·自序》<div id='poem_1320334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>集杜诗自序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320334")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320334'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320334'>余坐幽燕狱中，无所为，诵杜诗，稍习诸所感兴，因其五言，集为绝句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320334_comment'></div>久之，得二百首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320334_comment'></div>凡吾意所欲言者，子美先为代言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320334_comment'></div>日玩之不置，但觉为吾诗，忘其为子美诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320334_comment'></div>乃知子美非能自为诗，诗句自是人情性中语，烦子美道耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320334_comment'></div>子美于吾，隔数百年，而其言语为吾用，非情性同哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320334_comment'></div>昔人评杜诗为诗史，盖其以咏歌之辞，寓纪载之实，而抑扬褒贬之意灿然于其中，虽谓之史可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320334_comment'></div>予所集杜诗，自余颠沛以来，世变人事，槩见于此矣，是非有意于为诗者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1320334_comment'></div>后之良史，尚庶几有考焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1320334_comment'></div>岁上章执徐，月祝犁单阏，日上章协洽，文天祥履善甫叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1320334_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1320334'>是编作于前年，不自意流落馀生，至今不得死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1320334_comment'></div>斯文固存，天将谁属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1320334_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1320334_comment'></div>非千载心，不足以语此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1320334_comment'></div>壬午正月元日，文天祥书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1320334_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年1月</a>　正月二十后，卧病。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　本年春，作《赞》，拟终时书之于衣带间。作品：《自赞》<div id='poem_1320434' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1320434' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1320434?labeling=true' target='_blank'>自赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1282年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋末元初 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26406, "宋末元初", "文天祥", "poem_title_1320434")'>文天祥</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1320434_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1320434'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1320434'>吾位居将相，不能救社稷，正天下，军败国辱，为囚虏，其当死久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1320434_comment'></div>顷被执以来，欲引决而无间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1320434_comment'></div>今天与之机，谨南向百拜以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1320434_comment'></div>其赞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1320434'>孔曰成仁，孟云<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1320434", 1320434, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>取义</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1320434_comment'></div>惟其义尽，所以仁至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1320434_comment'></div>读圣贤书，所学何事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1320434_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1320434", 1320434, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>而今而后</span>，庶几无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1320434_comment'></div>宋丞相文天祥绝笔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1320434_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年4月8日</a>　本日有诗感怀。作品：《四月八日》<div id='poem_59040' class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_59040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_59040'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_59040'>今朝浴佛旧风流，身落山前第一州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_59040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_59040'>赣上瑶桃俄五稔，海中玉果已三周。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59040'>人生聚散真成梦，世事悲欢一转头。<div id='poem_sentence_2_59040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_59040'>坐对薰风开口笑，满怀耿耿复何求。<div id='poem_sentence_3_59040_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_59040'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_59040_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年4月</a>　本月，另有诗感怀。作品：《夜起》<div id='poem_59144' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_59144' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_59144'>一春花里离人泪，万里灯前故国情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_59144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_59144'>龙去想应回海岛，雁飞犹未出江城。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年5月</a>　本月回忆去年五月十八日之事,有诗感怀。作品：《己卯五月十八日》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年8月</a>　复求死以拒绝元廷欲图大用的诱降，谢昌元、王积翁诸人，以书谕意者也。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年</a>　元参政麦述丁建言杀文天祥，但元帝犹豫不决。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年12月9日</a>　出狱，临刑，向南一拜后从容就义。享年四十七。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1282&endYear=1282')">1282年12月10日</a>　本日元廷谕欧阳夫人收拾遗体，江南十义士奉柩葬都城小南门外五里道旁。<br /></div>
